New Spanish Cabinet Formed 72

Lerroux Appointed Prime Minister, Romero Appointed Foreign Minister: Three Cabinet Crises in Five Months

Madrid - After Lerroux had satisfactory discussions with the leader of the Agrarian Party, Valladares, he formed a new cabinet today. Eight cabinet members remained in their positions. The new additions were Romero as Foreign Minister, Alonso as Minister of the Interior, Spanish bank president Salazar as Minister of Finance, and the current ambassador to Paris, Madariaga, as Minister of Education. Since September of last year, this has been Lerroux's third cabinet formation. The first one only lasted three weeks because the Radical Party withdrew its support and it collapsed. The second one lasted from December 16th of last year to March 1st of this year because the Catholic Popular Action Party did not provide support and it resigned. (China Central News Agency Telegram, 3rd)

British House of Commons Discusses Boycott of Japanese Dumping 73

Prohibition of Imports of Goods Made by Forced Labor Feels Administratively Difficult

Private Bill Ultimately Not Established

London - The House of Commons today discussed a private member's bill dealing with imported goods. The bill aims to authorize the government to reject imports of goods made by forced labor. Conservative MP Williams asked the government to pay attention to the dangerous competition of manufactured goods exported from tropical countries, and especially to rubber shoes shipped from Malaya and Hong Kong, as their numbers have recently increased significantly. In addition, India is the most important supplier of steel that Britain needs and should be protected from competition. Conservative MP Lycett said that Britain recently ordered 100,000 pairs of shoes from Bata in India, and there are also 60,000 pairs of rubber shoes shipped from Hong Kong. Several Conservative MPs from the opposition party supported the bill. Overseas Trade Minister Colville replied that the government expressed sympathy for the bill, but it was administratively difficult to establish it. If the most-favored-nation treatment agreement is greatly reduced, it will inevitably cause major commercial disturbances and increase the number of unemployed people. The bill was ultimately not established. (Reuters Telegram, 2nd)

Since the Devaluation of the Dollar, European Cash Has Flowed to the United States 74

American Financial Circles Are Skeptical About the Silver Issue

London - Financial circles here issued a message saying that since the devaluation of the dollar, a large amount of cash has flowed out of European central banks in gold, the amount of which is quite alarming. However, because the dollar has depreciated too much, countries have no profit to be made, so cash is no longer flowing out. In total, since President Roosevelt's new monetary policy was implemented, the central banks of France, the Netherlands, and Switzerland have lost a total of about 325 million yuan in cash reserves, of which France accounted for 188 million yuan, the Netherlands accounted for 85 million yuan, and Switzerland lost about 22 million yuan. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Washington - Major political and financial figures here are quite skeptical about the silver issue. The Treasury Department plans to wait and see what happens after the gold proposal is implemented before resolving the silver issue, so it may not be discussed in time in this Congress. However, silver senators are doing their best to hope for its success, so there is again talk of proposing a neutral method these days, and there is much criticism of Treasury Secretary Morgenthau's recent statement. (National Telegram, 2nd)

Fascist Faction Will Further Investigate the Iron Minister

Tokyo, this afternoon, the government held an extraordinary cabinet meeting in the Lower House. Minister of Education Hatoyama formally submitted his resignation. The reason for his resignation, he stated, was that a cultural and educational flaw had been left, so he resigned to take responsibility. Prime Minister Saito immediately discussed with the cabinet members, and as a result, Minister of Education Hatoyama's resignation was approved alone, and the Prime Minister temporarily took over. (3rd, China League Electric)

Tokyo, at 5:00 PM this afternoon, former Minister of Education Hatoyama issued the following statement of resignation when the dismissal order was announced: "This time, regarding my actions, there has been discussion and the world has been in turmoil, which is very regrettable. The incident that became a problem is completely unfounded. It is hereby declared that if decisions on whether to stay or leave are made due to slander and false accusations, it would be very harmful to public morals and people's hearts. Therefore, I look back on this issue and deal with it with detachment, believing that it is a service to society.

The sacred educational community must always be as bright and clean as a mirror. Who can tolerate clouding it? There will inevitably be a time for resolution in the future, but I deeply feel the fact that it has been clouded, and I must quickly remove the responsibility. Therefore, from a broad perspective, I retire cleanly to renew the influence of the educational community, and think about the way of mutual love among compatriots. With a mind as clear as a mirror and still water, I humbly ask for a graceful retirement." (The following is omitted)

(3rd, Dentsu Electric)

Tokyo, the Japanese Minister of Education is temporarily held concurrently by the Prime Minister. However, Hatoyama represents the Seiyukai party in the cabinet and cannot be compared with Foreign Minister Uchida and Commerce Minister Nakajima. The Seiyukai party expects Prime Minister Saito to consult with President Suzuki in the near future regarding a successor to the Minister of Education. Due to the current political situation, which is still unfavorable to political parties, the Seiyukai intends to recommend its successor to temporarily extend the life of the Saito cabinet. However, the National League and the Araki-affiliated members of the Upper House intend to further pursue the Iron Minister Saneto, and the future of the Saito cabinet is still difficult to be optimistic about. Okamoto Disciplined, Disciplinary Issues Come to an End 82

Tokyo, at 1:23 PM today, the House of Representatives held a plenary session. After passing various legal bills, it deliberated on the issue of Okamoto Ichiji's speech. First, Chairman Shimada of the Inquiry Committee reported on the inquiry process and divided Okamoto's speech into three items: (1) Minister of Education Hatoyama had interceded with Iron Minister Saneto at the Bank of Taiwan to sell Imperial Rayon stock, and both ministers received generous gifts from both parties. (2) Minister of Education Hatoyama gave money to 130 members of parliament during the Mid-Autumn Festival and at the end of the year. (3) Minister of Education Hatoyama received a bribe of 50,000 yuan from Fujita, the manager of the Sakhalin Industries Company. Regarding these three points, each of the three parties expressed their opinions. Hamada, the Seiyukai Inquiry Committee member, represented the Seiyukai's opinion and denied that it was all slander and that there were no such facts. The Minseito party believed that the first and second items were still suspicious, but the third item was true. The National League believed that all three points were facts. Then, Hamada, Tanihara, and Noda represented their parties and expressed their opinions, and then the discussion ended. Chairman Shimada then made a decision on the three cases. The Minseito and National League's proposals could not be passed. The House of Representatives plenary session, based on the report of Chairman Shimada, conducted another roll-call vote. As a result, 206 votes considered it slanderous, and 120 votes affirmed that it was untrue. The Seiyukai, with the power of the majority party, denied the improper conduct of Minister of Education Hatoyama and decided to punish Okamoto Ichiji. The meeting adjourned at 7:00 PM. (3rd, China League Electric)

Disputes Between Russia and Japan Arise Again (Vladivostok Correspondence) 99

The disputed oilfields of Hulu District, which are under development, are being tendered for along the Russian coast this year. Because the Japanese bid was calculated at 32.5 sen per ruble, the Far East Fisheries Director of the Soviet Union considered this to be inconsistent with reality and declared the Japanese bid completely invalid. The bidding will be conducted solely by the people of the Soviet Union. In other words, the Japanese will not receive any of the 84 fishing areas currently being tendered. The Far East Fisheries Director of the Soviet Union holds that although this matter has not yet been formally approved by the Soviet Union Central Committee, it is theoretically and factually based. Firstly, regarding the exchange rate between rubles and Japanese yen in the fisheries aspect between Japan and the Soviet Union, it was agreed upon by Soviet Ambassador to Japan Troyanovsky and Japanese Foreign Minister Kijuro Shidehara. At that time, Japan still maintained the gold standard, and the Soviet Union also had a profound intention to develop trade with Japan. However, since Japan abandoned the gold standard in 1931, the value of the Japanese yen against foreign exchange has gradually decreased. Now that it is less than half of the gold parity, the Soviet Union's income will naturally suffer. The local finances are also greatly affected, so it is necessary to correct this. Secondly, the First Five-Year Plan has been quite successful, and foreign relations are gradually improving. With the aggressive advance of Japanese imperialists, appropriate countermeasures must be taken. Therefore, the Japanese bid was directly declared invalid.

Since the Far East Fisheries Director of the Soviet Union has declared his purpose, the Japanese side will naturally not accept it and will protest. The reasons held by the Japanese side are: (1) The exchange rate of the ruble was agreed upon by Ambassador Troyanovsky and Foreign Minister Shidehara in 1931, and it was determined that each ruble was worth 32.5 sen in Japanese yen. The Soviet Union unilaterally declared the abandonment of the exchange rate without consulting with Japan or waiting for Japan's permission, which is a violation of the agreement. (2) The right to bid for the lease of fishing areas in the Far East is jointly held by the people of Japan and the Soviet Union, and there is no difference. Now that the Soviet Union has unilaterally declared the Japanese bid invalid, it is a far cry from the Russo-Japanese Fisheries Treaty. Japan will never recognize this kind of differential treatment. Japan will argue with the Soviet Union based on the above reasons. This incident is even more intense than before. However, the Soviet Union has its consistent monetary policy. The price of the ruble against foreign exchange must be officially fixed by the National Bank. At the same time, the ruble is prohibited from leaving the country, and the secret carrying out of foreign currency will be confiscated. The entry of foreign currency is also subject to strict restrictions. Therefore, the Japanese claim of an exchange rate agreement has only one-sided reasons and cannot be compatible with the fundamental national policy of the Soviet Union. Therefore, this problem is not easy to solve. There is also the issue of oil extraction in the northern part of Sakhalin Island. In 1929, it was mined by the North Sakhalin Oil Company. Up to now, the invested capital is estimated to be about 5 million yen. The Japanese government's subsidy in 1932 was only 100,000 Japanese yen, and in 1933, it was only 230,000 Japanese yen. However, it costs 300,000 to 400,000 yen to drill an oil well, so the company's capital is very weak. The area that has been mined so far is only one-twentieth of the area with the right to try mining, and the area where the trial mining has been successful is only one place in northern Okha. Even if the Kaganingri district, where trial mining will be successful within this year, is included, the area is still very small, and the ore veins are poor, so there is little hope for the future. Recently, the Japanese side has planned to invest another 2.8 million yen of new capital to open seven new wells (six wells are currently under construction). However, if the northern Sakhalin Island oil fields are to be actively mined, at least 50 wells must be opened based on the part of the Japanese lease, and the capital required is 15 million to 20 million Japanese yen. Compared with the current situation, there is a world of difference. If we look at the Soviet Union's extraction of oil in this area, using the financial resources of its state-owned trusts, the current annual output is about 300,000 tons. After the Second Five-Year Plan, in 1937, the output will reach 1.2 million tons. Even if the Japanese North Sakhalin Oil Company is now working hard to increase production, the annual output is only 200,000 tons. There is also an urgent problem, that is, the Soviet-Japanese oil trial mining lease will expire in 1936. According to the current trend, the area of trial mining cannot be abandoned. Even if the trial mining has been successful, it will be subject to the strong resistance of the Soviet Union industry. Japan's ambition to seize oil will inevitably become an illusion (February 12, 1934).

Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Plans Border Transportation 100

Four Points: Highways, Waterways, Railways, and Aviation Will be Submitted to the Executive Yuan for Approval and Implementation, Beijing News The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission believes that the transportation in Mongolia and Tibet is obstructed, resulting in backward industries and culture. He Jian Reorganizes Hunan Province Finances 101

Provincial Government Meeting Approves Two Proposals, Changsha Correspondence In recent times, due to the withering of people's livelihoods and the exhaustion of tax revenue, the finances of Hunan Province and its counties have been extremely difficult. In order to strictly implement frugality, He Jian proposed a plan for reorganizing the income and expenditure of Hunan Province on February 13, which has been approved and implemented by the Standing Committee of the Provincial Government. Yesterday (27th) at 10:00 AM, the members and directors of the Provincial Government held the 441st Standing Committee meeting. He also temporarily submitted two major plans in writing for reorganizing the finances of Hunan Province and its counties. The attending members and directors unanimously approved and passed it, and it will be announced and implemented today (28th). The original plan is as follows: (1) No Additional Surcharges on Land Tax and Miscellaneous Donations are Allowed. It has been found that in recent years, the people's livelihood has reached the extreme point of withering. Although it is due to natural disasters such as floods and droughts, or the ravages of bandits and communists, the complexity of politics, the weight of taxes, and the frequent increase in supplies are also a major reason. The surcharges on land tax in various counties range from 18 or 19 yuan per official tax to 7 or 8 yuan at the least. The extraction is unlimited, but the people's strength is unsustainable. The cowardly are forced to flee, and the cunning therefore delay payment. The more urgent the collection, the deeper the people's suffering. In the end, the various undertakings that have been promoted either end halfway or fail to see success, so the huge sums of money spent on the preparations are also thrown into a void. If there is no change in course and rest for the people, the state of withering will be even worse than today. The Provincial Government, having seen this, specially dispatched the entire Provincial Committee in June of last year to tour various regions to investigate urgent matters and reduce them as appropriate. It has indeed been slightly reduced. However, later, various counties, due to insufficient funds, requested that the reduced surcharges be allowed to be restored, and some even submitted requests to increase them. If no restrictions are added, the additional surcharges will be endless. The Executive Yuan and the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission Nanchang Branch have repeatedly issued telegrams, stating that the rural economy is collapsing and we must seek revitalization, and ordered us to reduce or abolish the original land tax surcharges and various miscellaneous donations appropriately. Now that the local expenses of various counties have not been offset by other funds, it is difficult to sharply reduce the original surcharges. However, in the future, all undertakings that should be carried out should be based on the existing financial resources of the counties, and the plans should be considered, and they must not exceed the possible scope of the county's finances. Arbitrary expansion and requests to increase surcharges and various miscellaneous donations are not allowed, and the surcharges or donations that have been abolished are not allowed to be transferred for other purposes without authorization, in order to show restrictions. We must still find ways to save money and strive to gradually reduce them, so that the rural economy can gradually recover. Correspondingly, it is submitted to the general meeting and respectfully requests public decision. (2) The Expenses of Various Agencies Must Not Request Additional Funding. It has been found that in recent years, the country has been in turmoil, and natural disasters have occurred one after another. Hunan Province is located in a critical area and supplies are frequent. The people after the robbery have not yet recovered their vitality, the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, the people's strength is dwindling, and tax revenue is exhausted. It is impossible to find ways to increase revenue, and it is difficult to limit spending. Thinking about the past, I am always saddened. However, in times of worry and danger, we should encourage vigilance and sincerity. Loving the people is the way to save the country, and saving money is the way to love the people. In the future, the Provincial Government and the four departments of People's Finance, Construction, and Murder should share the purpose of benefiting the lower levels at the expense of the upper levels, cultivate a frugal and simple style, and weigh the importance of use. When spending, we must first measure the person. All expenses must strictly adhere to the budget. Even if there are any additional needs, they can only be saved from the original expenses and must not be arbitrarily proposed, nor can they be requested to be added afterward, so as to ensure that the people's strength is not exhausted and the official affairs are not closed. We must know that taking it has a limit, and it is even more important to use it sparingly. Saving a penny of financial resources for the people is to cultivate a share of vitality for the country. The way to govern lies in this. Therefore, a special case is submitted to the general meeting, respectfully awaiting the decision. (February 28)

Wuxi 104

Improving the Wuxi-Shanghai Road The Wuxi-Shanghai highway is a section of the Beijing-Shanghai National Highway. The section from Wuxi to Changshu was previously inspected by engineer Wang Yanquan from the Construction Department. The party, together with technician Jin Xinjing from the county government, started from Guangqin Road and inspected along the route for five days, passing through Dongting, Anzhen, and Guan Jian, and reaching the Changshu border. The existing route really needs to be improved and changed. A plan has been drafted to extend the starting point of the original route, Zhoushanbang, to Tonghui Road, in order to connect with the Xicheng and Xiyi roads. The second to twelfth curves of the original route, which are 4,450 meters long, should be changed to a straight line, which can reduce 250 meters of the concave in the roadbed. Also, if the entire road is improved, four bridges can be reduced, the route can be shortened by 900 meters, and the cost of other road surface construction and various vehicle consumption can be saved by 45,000 yuan. A description has been drafted and submitted to the Construction Department, ordering the county government to quickly remeasure, redraw the map, and carry out the work diligently.

Further Interrogation in the Bantang Temple Murder Case 105

An unidentified male corpse was found in Yanghuaibang, Bantang Temple, near Tangtou Town in the sixth district of the county. After the village head reported it, the county court prosecutor's office examined the body and found that it had been slashed in twelve places. The village head was ordered to prepare a coffin and enshroud the body, pending the arrest and investigation of the murderer. After extensive investigation, it was learned that the deceased was Hu Yutao, 23 years old, from Hujiawan, Jiangyin. He had two elder brothers, who were both in the cloth business. The deceased's behavior was always extremely romantic, so he was at odds with his family and eventually wandered outside. In the winter of the 19th year, he was arrested and imprisoned by the Jiangyin County for suspected counter-revolutionary activities. He was later rescued and released by fellow villagers. Although he later attended Qingdeng Middle School, he eventually dropped out due to his bizarre behavior. However, the county government's arrest warrant was not withdrawn, and he lived by borrowing money. This time, he was brutally murdered. Some say it was internal strife within the Communist Party, but it was actually a political assassination.

Zhengtong Steamer Damages Two Civilian Boats The fifth steamer of the Zhenxianban Zhengtong Company ran aground the other day while sailing from Zhenjiang to Xiannu. When it arrived at the Fifth Ferry of Xianzhen, the driver immediately reversed the wheel, mistakenly hitting and damaging two civilian boats, causing a dispute. After mediation, compensation was paid for repairs.

Fire Burns Down Gatehouse, Maid Falls and Gets Injured 107

At the home of Wei Zechang, a resident of Zuowei Street in Xincheng, Yangzhou, a fire broke out on the 2nd due to careless cooking, spreading to the accumulated firewood and reaching a raging state by about 4 pm. Fortunately, it was daylight, and various water associations arrived one after another to put out the fire. Several rooms upstairs and downstairs in the station house were burned down. In the midst of the chaos, a maid fell from the upstairs, injuring her vitals. Fortunately, she was rescued and sent to a nearby hospital for treatment, and her life is not in danger.

Zhenjiang 109

Verdict in the Lu Yaochang Embezzlement Case Lu Yaochang, the former accountant and technical director of the Peixian Construction Bureau, previously served as the director of the Construction Bureaus of Shanghai and Siyang counties. Last spring, while working at the Peixian Construction Bureau, he was accused by citizens of the county of embezzling public funds. The provincial government transferred the case to the court. After two months, the debate finally concluded a few days ago, and the verdict was announced yesterday. Lu Yaochang was sentenced to two years and ten months of imprisonment for continuously embezzling items held in his public office, and deprived of public rights for five years. The defendant should compensate the plaintiff in the incidental civil lawsuit for 3,752.55 yuan. After the verdict was announced, Lu Yaochang immediately stated in court that he was dissatisfied and requested an appeal.

Changshu 110

New Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce Elected The county's Chamber of Commerce held elections for supervisors and committee members last year, but the Silver Money Industry Association withdrew from the Chamber of Commerce due to suspected lottery fraud, and the re-election was suspended. Half a year has passed. Now, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has explained that the procedures are in compliance and issued a notification. After receiving the order, the county's Chamber of Commerce elected standing committee members and a chairman on March 1. County magistrate Zhou Heng personally attended the election, and the Party Department also sent committee members Shi Minyong and Wu Zhongying to guide the process. As a result, the former chairman, Pang Jiegong, was elected as the re-elected chairman, but Pang resolutely refused to take office due to the disputes of last year. After repeated persuasion from the committee members, he finally acquiesced.

Shao Beimei, a flirtatious woman from Sanjiao, Shuangsui Township, First District, is 23 years old and unmarried. She has had affairs with more than 20 men. This incident aroused opposition from the local people and caused a disturbance. Hangzhou 114

Couple Commits Suicide, One Dies, One Lives Xie Zhiwen, a 30-year-old pharmacist from a Shanghai Nanjing Road pharmacy, was from Jiaxing. His wife, Wang, was also from Jiaxing. They lived together in Shanghai. Unexpectedly, on February 5, he was accused of theft by the comprador and his business was suspended, and his deposit of 128 yuan was confiscated. Xie then came to Hangzhou with his wife, staying at the Cangzhou Hotel, planning another plan. However, because they were out of money and had no relatives, they had the idea of suicide. The couple took Lysol and went to the Yue Tomb area to jump into the lake in the middle of the night. They were discovered by the police and taken to the bureau. Seeing their changed expressions, they were sent to the Municipal Hospital for treatment overnight. After emergency treatment by the doctor, the man was out of danger yesterday. His wife, Wang, died at 12 noon because she had taken too much poison and could not be saved. The local court was notified, and prosecutor Chen Huaming led officials to examine the body and prepare a coffin.

The Hangzhou Garrison Command received a report from the Provincial Public Security Bureau that it had arrested Liu Jinkui, a robber who robbed the property of Xu Achuan, a resident of Baishi Temple. He was brought to the Garrison Headquarters with the stolen white silk and silk thread for interrogation. After interrogation, Liu confessed that he had robbed Xu Achuan's house and shared the white silk and silk thread. Xu Achuan, the victim, was also brought to the case and confirmed that the white silk was indeed the stolen property. His crime was unforgivable. He was sentenced to death according to law and submitted to the provincial government for approval. At 8 am yesterday (the 3rd), the criminal Liu Jinkui was identified and handed over to the Provincial Public Security Bureau and escorted to the scene of the crime for execution by shooting.

The Coroner is Beaten While Examining a Body Gong Xueqing, a child bride of Gu Falin in Shijia Town, First District, suddenly died a few days ago. The family of the deceased requested the county to send someone to examine the body. Coroner Deng went to the scene the day before yesterday (the 26th). Unexpectedly, the family of the deceased gathered more than a hundred people and surrounded Coroner Deng, forcing him to rule that she had been strangled to death. They tore Coroner Deng's clothes and injured his back, resulting in no conclusion and dispersing. Yesterday (the 1st), County Magistrate Zhang personally went to examine the body and led more than a dozen police officers to the scene to maintain order. The examination revealed injuries on the waist and back, and rope marks on the front and back of the neck. It remains to be proven whether she was strangled to death. Yesterday, Gu Falin turned himself in. After a brief interrogation by Coroner Deng, he was put in shackles and imprisoned.

Special Report

Impressions of the Economic Survey of Guizhou Province (5) Qian Jiaju 117

To return to the original topic, we spent a total of forty-eight days in Nanning. This month and a half was entirely consumed in referencing materials, compiling forms, dividing survey areas, and creating budgets. The most difficult part of our work was the lack of preliminary survey materials and the scarcity of existing reference materials. The gazettes of various departments and agencies, chapters, and magazine articles were not sufficient for us to create a survey plan. In addition, there were only some statistical data from the Statistics Bureau, that is, the manuscript prepared for compiling the Guangxi Yearbook. However, because the methods they used were indirect surveys rather than direct surveys, the bureau sent the prepared forms to the county political associations to be filled out by the county magistrates, so there were many questionable aspects to the materials. Mr. Yang Chuo'an has always advocated "rather be excessive than deficient" when it comes to statistical data, believing that "having something is better than having nothing." This is slightly different from our usual academic attitude. In this environment, the lack of preliminary survey data forced us to expand the scope of our work to include agriculture, industry, and commerce. We decided to organize a Guangxi Economic Survey Team, divided into three groups: agriculture, industry, and commerce. The agriculture group was led by Mr. Han Dezhang, the industry group by Mr. Wu Bannong, and the commerce and finance group was led by me. Each group recruited five to six to a dozen surveyors. Most of the surveyors were graduates of the Technical Personnel Training Institute run by the Statistics Bureau. They had received preliminary academic training in statistics and surveying. In addition, several colleagues from the Statistics Bureau also participated. Mr. Zhang Junmin and Mr. Liu Xuan (graduates of the Agricultural Department of Jinling University) participated in the agricultural group, and Mr. Yang Mingzhao and Mr. Liu Bingxin (graduates of Tsinghua University) participated in the industrial and commercial group. Our work plan was roughly as follows:

Agricultural Survey: The central questions are: in terms of crops, the emphasis is on the varieties, quality, output, cultivation methods, and costs of grain and important industrial raw materials; in terms of agricultural economics, the emphasis is on the production and consumption of farm households, farm household side businesses, the tenancy system, and rural finance. Survey areas: (1) the whole county, (2) Yangshuo, (3) He County, (4) Rong County, (5) Xiang County (6) Yishan, (7) Nandan (8) Teng County, (9) Yulin, (10) Binyang, (11) Guo [?])

De (12) Baise, (13) Longzhou

Industrial Survey: The central questions: This survey is divided into four aspects: (1) family industry, (2) scientific and industrial factories, (3) small factories using power, (4) new-style large factories. The issues to be emphasized are roughly divided into production relations, raw material supply, production costs, marketing conditions, labor livelihoods, and the rise and fall of various industries in recent years and the reasons, etc. In addition, the weaving industry is the most popular folk industry in Guangxi, but the clothing of the people of Guangxi still depends heavily on other provinces or overseas. [An investigation into the import of cotton, yarn and cotton cloth in recent years shows that it reaches] several tens of millions of dollars, which is the main reason why the trade surplus has increased year by year. This point deserves special attention and should be given special attention during the survey. Survey areas: (1) Nanning, (2) Wuzhou (3) Liuzhou, City, (4) Danghezhong, (5) Guilin, Lingchuan (6) Binyang, (7) Yishan) (8) Du'an (9) Yulin, (10) Rong County, (11) Pingnan, (12) Pingle, (13) Longzhou Commercial and Financial Survey: The central questions: In terms of commerce, the emphasis is on the commercial conditions, market conditions, sales of major items in various stores, profit and loss of operations, marketing of major import and export goods, and changes in prices, etc. In terms of finance, the emphasis is on the financial institutions, financial market conditions, currency system, and pawnshops in various places, etc. Survey areas: (1) Wuzhou, (2) Nanning, (3) Longzhou, (4) Baise, (5) Guilin, (6) Liuzhou, (7) Rubu (8) Guiping, (9) Pingle, (10) Yulin, (11) Guixian

After the work plan for the survey was decided, we began to make preparations for departure, such as purchasing folding beds, medicines, and setting up specimen collection boxes and printing various survey forms, etc. We had a total of eleven types of survey forms, each ranging from two or three pages to a dozen pages. Fortunately, our friend Mr. Lai Yanyu (Director of the Guangxi Printing Bureau) helped us greatly, so that the forms could be printed on schedule. This is something we are particularly grateful for in this survey.

But before I can actually go out on a survey, I have to talk about the languages of Guangxi. Originally, there are many dialects in various parts of China, not only differing from province to province and county to county, but also differing between the city and the countryside within a county. This is not only true in Guizhou Province, but Guangxi is undoubtedly the province with the most complex languages. They have what are called Mandarin, Baihua, Pinghua, Kehua, Konghua, Ronghua, Yaohua, Miaohua, [?hua], Guoguo hua, the variety of which is impossible to investigate, and each county has its own native dialect, which is not counted. We can say that no Guangxi person speaks all the Guangxi languages, just as no Chinese person speaks all the Chinese languages of the provinces. The most popular languages in Guangxi are Mandarin and Baihua. The so-called Mandarin is spoken in the Guilin and Liuzhou areas and is also called Guilin Mandarin. It is slightly flatter than Beijing Mandarin and is similar to Hubei and Sichuan dialects. Baihua is Cantonese. The reason why Cantonese is called "Baihua" is unknown. This type of Baihua is spoken in the Xijiang River basin and southern Guizhou Province, probably because it is close to Guangdong. In addition, Zhuanghua, Pinghua, and Hakka are also very influential. Often, several languages are used in one county. For example, Zhuanghua speakers account for about 60% of Liuzhou, while Baihua, Yuannan, and Hakka speakers each account for 10%. Nanning also uses Mandarin, Baihua, Pinghua, and Zhuanghua. It is almost non-existent for only one language to be used in one county. According to reports from civil affairs inspectors, the Guangxi Civil Affairs Association has produced a percentage comparison chart of various languages in Guangxi. According to the chart, Mandarin is spoken in 54.89% of the counties, Baihua is spoken in 62.22% of the counties, Hakka is spoken in 51.06% of the counties, Pinghua is spoken in 19.15% of the counties, local languages are spoken in 40.24% of the counties, Zhuanghua is spoken in 25.93% of the counties, Yaohua is spoken in 22.95% of the counties, Miaohua is spoken in 8.15% of the counties, and Tonghua is spoken in 2.22% of the counties. In total, they add up to 286.81%, which shows that each county uses an average of more than two languages. This time, we traveled to so many places and the distribution area was so sparse, so the difficulty of encountering language barriers was particularly serious. Fortunately, most of the surveyors we brought were from Guizhou Province, and they all spoke two languages, that is, Guangxi Mandarin and Baihua, and many could also speak Zhuanghua and Hakka. This problem was barely solved.

Carrying an Aircraft 127

It can also be equipped with three state-of-the-art machine guns. The flight speed is 150 miles per hour, which can be increased to 170 miles per hour. It can carry 600 gallons of gasoline. If it is converted into a commercial passenger plane, it can carry 15 passengers, 450 pounds of luggage, and 200 pounds of mail. The interior is very beautiful. The Cotton Industry Control Association Improves the Cotton Industry in Shaanxi 132

Purchasing more than 4,000 dan of cotton seeds for distribution in Shaanxi. Experts are dispatched to form a cotton industry improvement office. Since Shao Lizhi, chairman of the Shaanxi Provincial Government, took office, he has worked hard to resume work. Because Shaanxi Province has been suffering from droughts and floods for years, the people are struggling to survive. Although Shaanxi is the largest cotton-producing area in our country, it has been on the verge of bankruptcy in recent years. Therefore, he and the National Economic Commission's Cotton Industry Control Association jointly formed a cotton industry improvement office and are now starting to organize and distribute cotton seeds. The details are as follows:

Cotton Seeds Transported to Shaanxi 133

Since the National Economic Commission's Cotton Industry Control Association received the request from Shaanxi Province to jointly form a cotton industry improvement office with Shaanxi and requested to purchase good cotton seeds for distribution to farmers in various places in Shaanxi for planting, the Cotton Control Association has appointed a special commissioner to purchase them in Zhangde, Henan. A total of more than 4,000 dan have been purchased, with a purchase price of about 3 yuan and 5 jiao per dan, totaling more than 10,000 yuan, which is垫借 by the Cotton Control Association. The cotton seeds have been transported from Zhangde to Lingbao. The association has notified Shaanxi Province to send personnel to transport them to Shaanxi. However, Lingbao to Shaanxi still needs to go through the Lingtong section of the Longhai Railway, and the freight is very high. The Shaanxi Provincial Government is financially strained and unable to pay. The office is now requesting the Longhai Railway Bureau to transport the cotton seeds to Tongguan free of charge. The bureau is still considering it, so the cotton seeds are still滞留 in Lingbao.

Agricultural Cooperation 134

The Cotton Industry Improvement Office jointly formed by Shaanxi Province and the Cotton Control Association is now starting to organize. The National Economic Commission's Cotton Industry Control Association has appointed Xu Cudi, an expert from the Raw Materials Department, to conduct the work. After arriving in Shaanxi, it is also necessary to organize agricultural production cooperation enterprises so that farmers' produce will not be manipulated by merchants. Because the farmers in the area have been displaced since the disaster, their vitality has not recovered. Therefore, agricultural cooperation enables farmers to sell their crops at good prices, stabilize their lives, and gradually get them back on track. Mr. Xu studied in the United States and has a good understanding of cooperative undertakings. After returning to China, he engaged in cooperative undertakings and was the first to create China's cooperative movement. As for the date of Mr. Xu's arrival in Shaanxi, it has not yet been determined due to the many business matters to be discussed. Zou Bingwen may travel with him at that time.

International Trade Association Holds General Meeting Yesterday 143

The Chinese International Trade Association held its general meeting yesterday at the Bank Club. Members Liu Shimu, Zou Bingwen, Xu Xinliu, Wu Damu, Ren Sida, Li Shanshu, Guo Bingwen, Lin Kanghou, Luo Daojin, Sheng Zhuosan, and Qiao Wenshou, representing Zhejiang Industrial Bank, were present. Chairman Guo Bingwen reported on the association's activities, stating that international trade is the lifeblood of a nation's economy. In modern times, countries not only compete with each other with their full governmental power, but their people also pay absolute attention to promoting trade. China's trade deficit has been increasing year by year, reaching over 690 million yuan last year. The increasing deficit should be addressed. The association's mission is to develop foreign trade. Guo Bingwen and others were entrusted to preside over the association's affairs and wished to actively proceed. However, due to economic reasons, the original plan could not be completed, which they deeply regretted. The association's work can be simply divided into (1) investigation and research, (2) recommendations, and (3) communication. In investigation and research, the findings are printed into publications for the reference of various industries and scholars. There was a regular publication called "International Trade Weekly," but it was suspended in October of the 21st year due to lack of funds. There were also industry books such as "Directory of British, American, German, French, and Italian Trading Companies in China," "Survey of Shanghai Market Paper," "Export Guide," and "Procedures for Foreign Trade of Chinese Raw Silk." In terms of recommendations, they are either related to the interests of manufacturers or to national sovereignty, and are contributed whenever there are observations. For example, the current requirement for imported goods to be labeled with the name of the factory and place of origin is one of the association's recommendations. In terms of communication, there are many affairs such as cooperation matters, assistance in business, introduction, or reception, which are detailed in the report. In short, the association's mission is very important, especially under the current trade deficit situation. Special efforts should be made. On the occasion of the general meeting, a brief summary of past work is made. It is hoped that all comrades will unite more closely, continue to make progress, and determine the future direction to achieve the initial goals and complete the mission. Subsequently, the members discussed and passed the budget and several proposals, deciding to re-elect officers by means of communication. It is also heard that the association will amend its constitution to reduce membership fees in order to encourage participation from various industries and specialized scholars and enhance the effectiveness of research.

Ministry of Industry Orders Commodity Inspection Bureau to Conduct Hemp Export Inspection 144

To improve quality and maintain international credibility, the bureau is studying the order in detail. The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau received instructions from the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating that the Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureau reported that hemp is a major export of China. According to customs reports, in the past three years, the average annual export volume from Hankou was 232,518 dan of ramie, 68,247 dan of jute, and 19,286 dan of kenaf. Foreign trade occupies an important position. However, Chinese farmers and merchants do not know how to improve. The quality is impure, the grades are uneven, and there are often cases of adulteration and counterfeiting, and sulfur fumigation, which damages the strength. As a result, it is not welcomed by foreign merchants, and the export volume has been decreasing. In order to promote improvement and revive the rural areas, it is proposed to conduct hemp inspection, with detailed rules attached for reference. It is found that this item of hemp has been approved by the Ministry to be held, and a copy of the provisional rules is sent for reference and implementation. After receiving the order, the bureau has issued it to the Agricultural Products Inspection Office for detailed study, and is investigating the export volume of hemp in this port in order to start preparations.

Silk Weaving Industry in Extreme Decline, Factories Revise Wage Standards 145

To maintain the precarious situation by reducing original wages, the plan was filed with the party and government yesterday to avoid disputes. The Shanghai Silk Weaving Trade Association stated that the silk weaving industry has been affected by the recession, and the business is in extreme decline. It is difficult for factories to maintain operations. Therefore, the wage standards have been revised and submitted to the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau for record to avoid disputes. The original submission stated that the silk weaving industry is in extreme decline and on the verge of bankruptcy. It is requested to revise the wages according to precedents to maintain the precarious situation and be filed for record. It is true that the member factories are affected by the recession, and the business is extremely poor. Many factories are on the verge of bankruptcy. After the major shutdown last year, those that did not go bankrupt also suffered losses. The silk market relies entirely on profits from sales prices, but the rural areas in the country are bankrupt, the purchasing power is weak, and the impact of Japanese goods is even greater. As a result, the sales price has plummeted, and various products have fallen below the cost price, which is a huge amount. Manufacturers with limited capital cannot stand the unlimited losses and cannot stand firm. Although they tried their best to plan to start work this spring, they are uncertain about the future and have no good way to maintain operations. It is found that there were more than 700 looms in the city, and only more than 4,000 looms were operating in normal times. The number gradually decreased last year, and only more than 2,000 looms were working at the end of the year, and they were all struggling to make ends meet. The number of unemployed workers is more than 10,000. Those who try hard to start work are thinking about the livelihood of the workers, and digging flesh to mend sores does not benefit the investors in the slightest. For example, the silk factory suffers

losses due to stagnant sales and falling prices. Although it has tried its best to save expenses and reduce costs, the labor cost is still the biggest burden. Because the electric silk weaving industry has progressed from the hand weaving industry, its regulations

The wages are calculated on a piecework basis. When the electric silk weaving industry was first established, the two people were not familiar with the machinery and produced less, so the wages were similar to those of the hand weaving industry. Later, the machinery became skilled, the efficiency was improved, the workers' skills advanced, and the output increased greatly, but the wages were still the previous standards. Therefore, the wages of the silk weaving industry in this city have always been the highest record of wages in various industries in this city. In the past, when the sales price was high, it could barely be maintained. Until last year, the price of goods fell sharply, and the wages remained the same, which is obviously unreasonable. For example, the most common weaving products in this city, He Shi crepe, each piece of labor costs an average of more than one yuan. In the past, the sales price of each piece was more than 20 yuan, and the labor cost accounted for about 5% of the cost. Recently, the sales price of each piece has fallen to 10 yuan, less than half of the original price, and the labor cost has not decreased, so it must account for 12% of the sales. As for the workers' output, it was less than one piece a day in the past, and recently it has doubled, and the workers' wages have increased a lot, but the factory has suffered losses, resulting in the silk weaving wages in this city, and

The cost of living is absolutely contradictory, and those who can fortunately avoid bankruptcy, can they get it? The member factories, in this turbulent autumn, think of the importance of the national production industry, and do not want to see the complete bankruptcy of the silk weaving industry. They only have to endure the pain and struggle, and try their best to save on all expenses. For unreasonable wages, they have to try to reduce them within the possible range. It is found that several member factories have been mediated by the Social Affairs Bureau and established in the winter, including: the wage for single crepe is 2.8 cents per yard, 6.2 cents for satin, 4.7 cents for double crepe, and 5.2 cents for jacquard machine.

The preparation wage is from 80 cents to 85 cents, and the after-wage is calculated at 85% of the original wage, which is still fair. The member factories of the association intend to revise the wage standards based on the above-mentioned wage settlement case, and respectfully request your Ministry (Bureau) to approve the record, so as to avoid disputes and maintain the precarious situation. This is for the public convenience. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau, the Municipal Party Department, and Wang Shiqiang, Chairman of the Shanghai Electric Silk Weaving Trade Association.

Reasons for Disciplinary Action Against Relief Personnel in Northern Anhui 147

Not due to Malpractice or Negligence. According to a report from the Guowen News Agency, regarding the case of disciplinary action against relief personnel in northern Anhui, the spokesperson of the National Government's Flood Relief Committee said yesterday that the case occurred in the autumn of the 21st year of the Republic of China. Supervisors Gao Yihan and others listed four main points of impeachment, including short-weighted sales, delayed flour production, and accused Quan Shaowu, Yang Shucheng, Cha Liangzhao, De Zhiruizhi, and Xin Boshen of suspected embezzlement and negligence. After more than a year of investigation by the Central Public Servants Disciplinary Committee, it was found that the impeached sections of short-weighted sales and delayed flour production were not due to malpractice. De Ruizhi and Xin Boshen were not subject to disciplinary action. However, official Quan Shaowu was given a reprimand, and Yang Shucheng and Cha Liangzhao were each given a demerit. The general idea of the disciplinary committee's decision was that (1) the sale of wheat flour was to meet the needs of the flood relief committee, and it was affected by the war in Shanghai at that time, not limited to the wheat relief in northern Anhui. The sale of wheat prices was carefully compared in Shanghai and was higher than the wheat prices purchased by import merchants from various countries at the same time, and there was no untrue or incomplete situation. (2) The short-weight item was not that the relief personnel in northern Anhui arbitrarily adopted weights and measures. There was a difference in the weights and measures, and there was a definite purpose. The profits and losses were all within the total income and expenditure of wheat relief, and no one could encroach on it. (3) For the flour production item, the US wheat in the US was converted into 72.6 pounds per hundred pounds. This time, 80 pounds of US wheat was converted into flour per hundred pounds, and there was no objection in each disaster area. Northern Anhui was a misunderstanding, and it was stopped as soon as it was opposed. (4) Regarding the delay item, the Flood Relief Committee sent Quan Shaowu as the special commissioner of relief in northern Anhui in early April. The people in the disaster area did not understand the facts and the relief process, and it was inevitable to misunderstand. The above four points are the actual situation of the disciplinary committee's decision on this case.

The committee has decided that there is no malpractice or negligence in the original four impeachment points. The truth is here. As for Quan Shaowu's

The reprimand was given because he was too strong and his measures were inappropriate. Yang Shucheng's two demerits were given because he argued with others and did not stop the relief transport and knew there was private but did not know there was public. Cha Liangzhao's demerit was given because he was the director of the emergency relief office and did not ask for help to stop selling Beng wheat due to the special circumstances in northern Anhui. The above points are the reasons why the officials should be punished. The outside world is unclear about the truth of this case, and the reports are diverse, which can easily lead to misunderstandings. Now that the facts have been proven, it is clear that this case is not related to embezzlement or malpractice.

銀行聨合準備會委員銀行代表大會（續前）] 152

Business Report: The decline of our nation's rural economy, the desolation of industry and commerce, and the gradual encroachment of internal strife and external threats intensified by the twenty-second year. We bankers, faced with this difficult and precarious situation, have adhered to a prudent policy, developing in an orderly manner. On the one hand, we have restored the original purpose of public organizations, and on the other hand, we have collectively strengthened their foundations and promoted their progress. Over the past year, joint reserves have become increasingly substantial, and the results of check clearing have been quite remarkable. What we advocated and hoped for more than a decade ago, and repeatedly discussed without success, has now been achieved in less than two years. This shows that matters that are truly needed by the world, and that are entirely beneficial without any drawbacks, may not be timely at first, but will ultimately achieve their goals. However, as mentioned above, the country's situation is difficult and perilous, and the global economic panic has reached its peak. The arms race among the great powers has intensified, and the issues in the Pacific and the Far East are showing signs of escalating tensions. Shanghai, as an international market, has very significant interests at stake with various countries. Any international change, whether political, military, or economic, is enough to affect and shake Shanghai's financial markets like a sudden thunderclap. If a global state of peace cannot be maintained, then the impact and shock will be unimaginable. From the very beginning of its establishment, this association has had a specific and detailed plan for how to expand its group and increase its strength in the future to meet this future crisis. We deeply rely on our colleagues to plan ahead and provide timely advice so that this association can follow a path. We cannot express enough our sincere prayers. As we reach the end of the twenty-second year's financial settlement period, we respectfully present the following summary report on the business situation over the past year: (A) Department of Joint Reserves (1) Admission of New Member Banks: In September of this year, China & South Sea Bank, The China Industrial Bank, China National Goods Bank, and The China Enterprise Bank simultaneously joined this association as member banks. Their voices were heard and their aspirations were met, greatly expanding the plan. The future of this association is promising. (2) Reserve Assets: The reserve assets deposited by various banks are mainly in the form of real estate and foreign securities. In January of this year, this association decided to include domestic government bonds as one of the types of reserve assets, considering that they were reliably guaranteed and had stable market prices after the implementation of the reorganization plan. At the same time, for the sake of extra stability, the percentage was restricted and the discount was reduced. The total amount of all reserves was 68.54% of the evaluated value in the previous financial settlement and 66.76% of the total evaluated value in the following financial settlement. According to the numbers in the following financial settlement, the breakdown of assets is: real estate accounts for 82.63% of the total, foreign securities account for 11.41%, and domestic government bonds account for 6.96%. (3) Various Documents and Interbank Lending and Discounting: The use of various certificates issued by various banks, in addition to being used as reserves, has increased compared to last year. However, the public certificate has been very scarce in circulation since its issuance last year. Considering that the original public certificates were limited to immediate payment and whole-number denominations, and based on our observations, they did not fully meet commercial needs, this association revised the public certificate regulations in May of this year and changed the design of the public certificates. While maintaining the characteristics of stability and reliability, we also endowed them with the functions of flexibility and convenience. At the same time, we increased the public certificate payment fund and changed the percentage of certificates issued, with public certificates and treasury bills each accounting for half. All of these changes took effect on July 4. By the end of the year, various banks gradually began to use the new public certificates externally. In the future, as this becomes a habit, it will definitely be beneficial to commerce. The revised public certificate regulations clearly stipulate the public certificate discounting method, so that it can complement interbank lending and achieve a regulatory effect. However, in Shanghai, the amount of silver deposited has increased from 430 million to 540 million, and the surplus capital is overflowing and congested. In this abnormal state of urban finance, the full implementation of the above-mentioned measures requires waiting and watching for a different day. After the implementation of check clearing, it was stipulated that the payable balance of each bank in one type of currency could be offset by deposits in other types of currency and transferred to the association for interbank lending. This has been done several times and has been quite convenient. (4) Exchange Bank Deposits: With the implementation of check clearing, each bank opened a current account at this association to receive and pay the exchange difference. At the end of the year, the total amount of deposits was 120 million silver dollars, of which silver dollars accounted for 42.25% and silver transfer dollars accounted for 57.75%. The concentration of funds means a thicker preparation, which is not only convenient for pastor's relief. (B) Department of Check Clearing (1) Summary of Affairs: This has been entrusted by the Shanghai Banking Association to handle check clearing matters. After five months of research and discussion, by the end of the year, preparations were completed. Thirty-two fellow institutions joined as exchange banks. On January 10 of this year, the check clearing house was officially opened. From the same day, the silver dollar check exchange was held. The total exchange on that day was 2,150,164.26 yuan, with 1,247 checks, which was the beginning of our country's exchange record. At that time, silver taels had not been abolished, and there were as many as four types of currencies commonly used in Shanghai. Because this association was a new initiative, it was planned that the check exchange of various currencies should be implemented step by step in order to proceed smoothly. On February 1, the silver transfer check exchange was added. On February 16, the silver tael check exchange was added. On March 1, the silver transfer tael check exchange was added. In order to suit actual needs, the originally scheduled exchange time was slightly changed, and the exchange site was moved from the association hall to the central hall. On March 1, the total exchange was 18,718,748.17 yuan, with 1,399 checks. The check exchange of the four currencies was thus fully completed.

On March 16, 56 branches of various banks in the city all joined the exchange, with the head offices of each bank acting as agents. The scope of the exchange was expanded from the urban area to the city area, and the convenience for each bank increased daily, and the function of the exchange became increasingly apparent. On April 6, the Shanghai banking industry was ordered by the Ministry of Finance to abolish the receipt and payment of silver taels. On the same day, the association abolished the silver tael and silver transfer check exchanges. By this time, the exchange business had become increasingly skilled, and the simplification of currency units from complex to simple gave the exchange a double benefit. The long-standing abnormal currency system was resolutely abolished. This is also what was previously said: "What is truly needed by the world, and is entirely beneficial without any drawbacks, will eventually achieve its goal." In the second half of the year, China & South Sea Bank, The China Industrial Bank, and China Enterprise Bank simultaneously joined this association as exchange banks. In addition, many fellow silver and money dealers entrusted exchange banks to collect checks on their behalf. Shanghai's financial habits, such as the different procedures for interbank collection and remittance, the different times for collection and remittance, the different habits of check payment, and the difference between transfer checks and head checks, have a very long history. This association handles check clearing and wants to bring these complex and divergent old habits into a neat and unified new order. We dare not close the door and build a car, nor can we cut our feet to fit the shoes. From planning to implementation, from implementation to progress, the difficulties in the process are innumerable. Our colleagues deeply know that these difficulties are the inevitable stage of a new business. Openness, honesty, and cooperation have made all the reforms smooth over the past year. (2) Exchange Volume: The total exchange volume for the whole year was 1,666,451,761.83 yuan, with 900,260 checks. The average exchange volume was 6,576,761.74 yuan, with 3019 checks. Comparing the monthly amounts, the exchange volume increased from more than 2 million per day from January to April to more than 5 million. The gradual expansion of the exchange scope can be seen here. The records for each month thereafter have increased. By October, the exchange volume exceeded 9 million yuan. In November and December, the exchange volume was also more than 8 million yuan. Since April, the number of checks collected by various banks on behalf of others has increased daily, and the joining of new exchange banks has increased the scope of the exchange in tangible and intangible ways. This is the main reason for the increase in the exchange volume. Other factors, such as the gradual increase in commercial receipts and payments and the development of various banks' businesses, are also related to the increase in the exchange volume. However, the current exchange figures only account for a part of the city's receipts and payments. It can only be used as a rough estimate of financial trends. The ratio of the exchange difference to the total exchange volume was 40.16% in March. After the abolition of silver taels, it gradually decreased, and it was only 27.06% in December. The effect of shrinking currency can be seen here. (3) Exchange Expenses: Exchange expenses are shared by various banks in proportion to the total amount of receipts and payments for the whole year. Each 1,000 yuan of exchanged checks requires a fee of 1.1 cents. The savings in labor costs for fellow businesses compared to the past are not limited to the above-mentioned ratio. In recent years, China's silk industry has been declining due to the dumping of foreign artificial silk. However, since last year, it has been able to rebound slightly due to the patriotism of the Chinese people. According to Mr. Wu Zhihao, after China's silk industry failed in Korea and Southeast Asia due to the dumping of Japanese artificial silk, it also became very sluggish in the country. However, since last year, Chinese silk has gained the trust of the Chinese people, resulting in a surge in purchasing power, increasing by 20% compared to previous years. Taking the Shanghai National Goods Company, which I run, as an example, the single item of silk crepe has also reached 700,000 yuan. The reasons for this are: (1) Chinese silk is cheaper, with prices more than half as cheap as in previous years. (2) Chinese silk has novel colors and patterns. Since last year, the colors and patterns of Chinese silk have been truly superior to those of artificial silk. (3) The cost of Chinese goods is low. Last year, silk prices were cheap, so the purchase price of silk was also low. The best-selling Chinese products are Hangzhou silk satin, followed by Shengze lake crepe and Shanghai's own factory silk. When asked about the company's plans for this year's national goods business, he said that the plans that are currently being planned and are about to be realized are the establishment of the Nanjing National Goods Company, as well as holding a North China Exhibition, that is, promoting in Tianjin, Beiping, Shanxi, Gansu, Qinghai, and other places, and also planning to form 100 national goods sales teams, divided into four locations. Seven-Year-Old Girl Tragically Burned to Death 156

Mother Orders Girl to Watch the Home While Buying Vegetables, the Stove Fire Ignites Clothing, and She Dies a Martyr; Fortunately, the Seven-Month-Old Infant is Safe

Fan Fei, a shareholder of the He Xing Hing Army Bed Shop at No. 643 Edward Road, French Concession, is a native of Jiangxi and is 31 years old this year. His wife, Xing, is 30 years old this year. They have one son and one daughter. The daughter's name is Kaihua, and she is 7 years old this year. The son is 2 years old. In fact, he was just born and barely seven months old. The family rents accommodation in the room behind the hall at No. 649, the fourth door next door to the west of the shop. Fan himself works in the shop and goes out early and returns late. Two days before, Fan got up and went to work in the shop. His wife, Ren, felt that it was cold in the morning, so she made a stove to cook breakfast. However, she did not put it out immediately. At about 9 o'clock, Ren placed the infant in a wooden sleeping bucket in the room and asked the girl Kaihua to accompany him by the side. At this time, the charcoal fire in the stove was just glowing. The girl happened to be standing next to the stove with her back to the stove and her face towards the wooden bucket in which the child was sleeping. Unexpectedly, the lower corner of the back of her cheongsam happened to be covering the fire on the stove, causing the corner of the cheongsam to be ignited. The girl did not know it until the fire rose and burned through her underwear, causing pain to her flesh. She then realized it and cried loudly and ran to the bed. However, the fire on her clothes was raging, causing it to ignite the bed curtains. At that time, neighbors mistakenly thought that the child was being beaten and cried, and did not pay attention. It was not until flames burst out of the door and the room was filled with smoke that Mrs. Zhu He, a Suzhou woman living on the upper floor behind the residence, discovered the fire. She ran down to check and saw that the bed curtains were completely on fire, and the girl was also covered in flames. She immediately called neighbors to come and put out the fire with water. However, the girl's clothes had all turned to ashes, and her flesh had also been burned. Because the fire toxins attacked her heart, she immediately fell to the ground and died. However, the seven-month-old infant was fortunately unharmed. When the child's mother, Fan Ren, returned home after buying vegetables,

the girl was already dead and could not be saved. She immediately reported to the French police station, who sent detectives to investigate. They then sent the body to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall morgue. Yesterday morning, they reported to the Second Special District Local Court and commissioned Prosecutor Wang Ren to come to the morgue to examine the body. It was determined that the deceased girl, Fan Kaihua, had been burned to death before her death. After questioning the child's mother, Fan Ren, and the witness, Zhu He, the body was sent to the family for burial.

The court approved the request. Lawyer Jiang continued, "Currently, the police station is prosecuting the two defendants, Dong and Wu, for attempted murder under Article 282, Section 2 of the Criminal Code and robbery under Article 348. However, the reason why the defendants wanted to rob the plaintiff was only recently found out by the police station. It turned out that the defendants had learned in advance that the plaintiff would carry a large sum of money to his office at the end of each lunar month to distribute wages. This time, he was carrying 20,000 yuan in cash and silver dollars, so they carried out the robbery on January 31. Unexpectedly, the loot was very small." the child, so I quickly declared in imperfect Shanghai, "This child is the son of my chief steward and is very poor." Then, I reached into my pocket

and took out a watch and gave it to them, saying, "This watch is very expensive and can be pawned for more than a hundred yuan." I also hugged the child from the front to the back and hid him inside my coat. I was afraid that they would continue to shoot, so I threw a blanket on my arm to prevent accidents. After traveling for a long time, the car had reached Avenue de la Victoire in the French Concession. I was deeply afraid that further resistance would endanger my life, and one bandit pointed his finger at my head and pulled the trigger. Fortunately, the bullet was jammed and did not come out, otherwise it would have been unimaginable. So I gave them a wallet containing 250 yuan in cash and silver dollars. At that time, because the road was uneven, the car slowed down. I took this opportunity, hugged the child, opened the car door,

Hebei Native Association General Meeting 161

The Hebei Native Association in Shanghai will hold its general meeting today (the 4th). The association has already notified all members to attend. Furthermore, after the association telegraphed its opposition to the Tianjin Municipal Finance Bureau's increase in brokerage tax, the Guangdong Native Association also sent a telegram in support. The original telegram is as follows: To Chairman Huang of Beiping and Chairman Yu of the Tianjin Provincial Government, We have learned that setting up checkpoints to collect brokerage taxes on fresh goods violates the municipal brokerage tax regulations. Moreover, collecting transit taxes on southern fresh goods that have already paid national taxes, forcing them to operate without brokers, is essentially a disguised form of likin. Sugar cane and oranges are special products of Guangdong Province, and your province is the only major market for their sale. Now, Tianjin merchants have suspended operations, and with the approach of warm spring weather, these goods are easily susceptible to spoilage. If transportation is not urgently resumed, the people of Guangdong will face starvation. We, as merchants, are appealing on behalf of the people. We humbly request that your esteemed chairman order the cessation of brokerage tax collection and instruct the Finance Bureau to find alternative solutions. We implore you to alleviate the suffering and allow normal transportation, so as to relieve the plight of the people and ease the difficulties of merchants. We will be eternally grateful and await your reply. Tang Haian, Chairman of the Guangdong Native Association in Shanghai, bows in winter.

Huihang Travel Agency Expands Organization 162

Renamed Zhejiang-Anhui Travel Agency, Automobile Department Already in Operation. Huang Yusheng, Wu Mingxin, Cao Zhigong, and others, Hui merchants in Shanghai, recognizing the increasing number of Hui people traveling back and forth after the opening of the Hangzhou-Hui road, joined forces with Hong Peiwen, Jiang Qingquan, and other Hui merchants in Zhejiang to establish the Huihang Travel Agency, seeking to provide convenient travel for fellow Hui natives. Now, with the increasing development of transportation between Anhui and Zhejiang provinces, extending beyond just the Hangzhou-Hui route to roads like Chuntun and Sutun, which are also slated to open soon, the organizers convened a meeting the other day and decided to expand the organization, renaming it the Zhejiang-Anhui Travel Agency. To meet the needs of fellow natives, the Hangzhou branch was established first. The agency address has been fixed at No. 46 Wushan Road, West Lake, Hangzhou. Six new-style automobiles purchased in Shanghai have been transported to Hangzhou for use. Therefore, the Automobile Department is already in operation, with low prices and convenient services that have been widely praised by travelers. The Shanghai office is temporarily located at the Huining Native Association, No. 21 Hongxiang Lane, Xinzha Road. Fellow natives who have inquiries can contact the office for introductions.

Shao Zenghua Lectures on Production Management 163

The China Industrial and Commercial Management Association held its 46th luncheon discussion meeting yesterday at the Linhua General Association on Beijing Road. Attendees included Li Zhaohuan, Fang Yexian, Tu Zheyin, Cheng Shouzhong, Chen Bingzhang, Pan Yangyao, Cao Yunxiang, Fang Xijian, Guan Renshi, Song Peidao, and over forty others. During the meeting, Shao Zenghua was invited to lecture on production management. A member of the Bingxun Stenography Agency was dispatched to record his speech, which stated in brief: Production management is a major branch of scientific management. Scientific management is the answer to problems in industry and commerce. The goal of industry and commerce is to make profits, so scientific management is the way to pursue profits. Profits can be pursued by expanding sales and reducing costs. Setting aside the former for the moment, the method of reducing costs can be divided into obtaining cheap raw materials and reducing manufacturing expenses. How to reduce manufacturing expenses is the task of production management. As for the method, there are roughly three aspects of savings: labor, raw materials, and machinery. Although the goals of production management are the same, the systems adopted vary. It is impossible to determine which is right or wrong. The key is for each factory to properly assess the situation, adopt legal methods, and then achieve the goal of profit.

Deaf-Mute Qiu Minrong Robbed on the Road 166

Truly, it is a case of suffering without being able to speak. Qiu Minrong, a 22-year-old Cantonese man, was born deaf, mute, and with a limp in one leg. His parents died early. At the age of ten, he entered the Shanghai West School for the Blind and Deaf. Because of his sincerity and diligence in his studies, he was deeply valued by the school authorities and teachers. After graduating, he was retained by the school as a teaching assistant, receiving a monthly allowance of $18. In addition to assisting with school affairs, Qiu was also responsible for collecting donations from various places. The other day, it was again time to collect this year's donations. Qiu left the school at 1:00 PM and went to the China Merchants Securities Exchange and Hengshun Bank on Sanma Road, where he collected a total of $275. After completing his task, he planned to return to the school to report. However, as he was walking near Pingliang Road, three thugs resembling workers suddenly jumped out from the roadside and blocked his path. One of the thugs stepped forward and snatched the leather bag from Qiu's hand. Then, they also seized the $18 salary and 14 cents he had just received from Qiu's pocket. Qiu was initially panicked, but seeing that none of the three had guns, he desperately gave chase, but was unable to call for help. At this moment, a car suddenly drove towards him. Qiu tried to stop it for rescue, but the car turned east without stopping. Seeing this, the three thugs feared that encountering another vehicle or passerby would lead to their capture. So, they turned back, knocked Qiu to the ground, and used iron pliers and files to beat him severely. As a result, Qiu was knocked unconscious. The three thugs fled without a trace. About a quarter of an hour later, a car passed by. The people in the car saw Qiu dressed neatly, lying in the middle of the road, so they got out of the car and helped him up. After questioning him in detail, they realized he was a deaf-mute. After Qiu explained in detail with a pen, they learned that he had been robbed. The people in the car then escorted him back to the school. It is reported that Qiu suffered serious injuries and will be hospitalized for treatment.

Apprentice Robbed While Buying Silver Coins, Never Returns 167

Was it fear of responsibility or a disappearance? Chen Zongwen, the owner of the Xie Xing cigarette and paper shop on Wutong Street in the city, reported to the police that his apprentice Huang Baolian (17 years old, from Chongming) was ordered to go to the tea market at 9:00 AM yesterday morning with $30 in paper money to buy silver coins. Unexpectedly, on the way, two robbers in the middle of the road robbed the apprentice of the paper money on him and pushed him to the ground. However, after Huang Baolian got up, he desperately chased after the robbers and did not return until late at night. The shop owner Chen Zongwen did not see the apprentice return at lunchtime, realized something was wrong, and went to search for him. He learned from bystanders that Huang Baolian had been seen chasing the robbers and falling to the ground. The shop owner Chen Zongwen did not dare to speculate whether the apprentice was afraid of being held responsible and did not return to the shop or whether he disappeared while chasing the robbers. Therefore, he wrote a report and submitted it to the Second Precinct of the First District, asking them to pay attention and investigate.

On September 27th of last year, at about 7:00 PM, the home of Yuan Cao, a woman living at No. 42 Hele Lane, Xinzha Road, was robbed of valuables worth $314. The Hongkou Police Station subsequently arrested the perpetrators Zhang Baocheng, Zhang Zirong, Chen Haiqing, and three others, and also arrested Fan Xiaomei for the separate crime of luring and selling women for profit. They were sent to the First Special District Court, where they confessed that their accomplice, Zhou Hailin from Jiangbei (who is blind in his right eye), had also participated in the robbery. Zhang and the other three have been sentenced to various terms of imprisonment. The other day, Min Huihai, a Chinese detective from the Disui Road Police Station, learned that the perpetrator Zhou was hiding at a certain address on Taipingqiao Road, Gaochang Temple, in the Nanshi area. He reported this to the chief detective, who, along with the Western detective Weitemi, went with detectives from the local Public Security Bureau to arrest Zhou and bring him back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Public Works Department, stated the previous circumstances and said that the defendant did not confess at the police station, but his blindness in the right eye matched the description provided by Zhang Baocheng. He asked for a postponement to investigate further. The defendant firmly denied the charges, saying that he had always been a small fruit vendor and knew nothing about the case. He asked for leniency. Judge Wu Zehan ordered that he be remanded in custody and that the matter be investigated and verified at a later date.
