Letters to the Editor 178

To the esteemed editor, I am writing to you regarding an article published in your newspaper on the 24th of this month, which stated that in a document submitted to the Ministry of Industry, it was stated that in November of last year, a document was prepared with attached drawings and specifications, and submitted to the Central Industrial Testing Institute of your ministry, requesting a fair evaluation and a certificate so that funds could be raised to complete the entire project and put it to practical use. Although several submissions have been made, no reply has been received. It is very confusing. There is a slight discrepancy between the news and the facts. According to us, we did not directly submit the document to the Ministry of Industry or the Central Industrial Testing Institute. However, the drawings and specifications were sent to Mr. Chen Xuanren of the institute on December 6 of last year for forwarding. The reason why it has not been approved so far is that, according to a letter from Mr. Chen, the matter is a private exploration, and the procedures are not formal, resulting in delays. The matter concerns the reputation of the year. In addition to writing to the institute to clarify the misunderstanding, we are writing to you specially to request a correction. We wish you all the best. Sincerely, Dan Chunqiao and Chen Xinbiao, inventors of the self-powered engine. March 3.

To the editor, Regarding the article in your newspaper on the 2nd of this month concerning the dismissal of Min Luobing, a candidate for the executive committee of this association, it stated that he was denounced to the Central Party Headquarters, and after the Party Headquarters sent personnel to investigate on the ground, it was found that Min had mishandled the strike at the Wusong Machinery Factory on the two railways, so he was specifically ordered to be dismissed and investigated. This is not consistent with the facts. I hope you will check and correct it. Sincerely, The Executive Committee of the Special Party Headquarters of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways. March 3.

To the editor, Today, your newspaper's local news section published a report on our association's representative meeting yesterday. There are still some mistakes, please correct them as follows: (1) Chairman of the Committee: Committee Member Runqing requested leave due to business, so the Standing Committee Member served as chairman. (2) The discount for February is 2.95%, starting from February 18, because that day was the first day of business after the end of the 22nd year of the general manager's term. Please publish this letter in the letters section as a correction to avoid misunderstanding. Sincerely, The Shanghai Money Trade Association, March 3, 23rd year of the Republic of China.

Reading and Writing Q&A 179

Reading and Writing

Reading Guidance··

At this moment, although I am writing this letter with great excitement, hoping that you will instruct me on how to solve these self-study difficulties, I am afraid that my requests will exceed the scope set by your department, or that you will not answer my request, right? Therefore, although I write at length and continue to hold the pen, I am somewhat worried. But I don't know if you will really abandon me and not reply? Probably not, right? I think so.

Sir! Like Zhou Yun, who published in the "Reading Q&A" column the day before yesterday, I am a person who has faith in new literature and has creative ambitions; and I am also a person who graduated from elementary school and dropped out of school without any written foundation; and my environment is exactly the same as Zhou's. I am a shop assistant, facing time constraints, and only have two precious hours of free time from 8:00 PM to 10:00 PM to work freely as much as possible. In these two extremely precious hours, although I have the wish to never give it up casually, when I review what I did in these two hours in the past, it is really a bit difficult to believe myself. Zhou Jun once said: "Comparing the results of unknowable future efforts with the emptiness of the past and present, it really makes me a bit dazed! In difficult and irregular self-study, the brain often shows confusion..." and also said: "...sometimes even too lazy to look up the dictionary, and there is no way to ask about places that cannot be understood. Just like this, just like this, time flies, and age increases, what achievements are there? Emptiness, confusion!" These few words of self-confession are indeed a true reflection of me! When I read Zhou Jun's letter, what made me feel even more ashamed was that Zhou Jun modestly thought that in irregular self-study, being able to jump from the level of an elementary school student to being able to write a decent letter with fluent and orderly words was comforting enough, but when I reviewed my so-called self-study in the past, it really made me lose the courage to recognize myself more deeply. (To be continued)

Laks was the opposite, with defense exceeding offense. Goalkeeper Kirklen made many excellent saves. His merits and demerits were half and half, only because he was not calm enough, which led to mistakes. Qinsheng Logan, the defender, and center-back Samos were very experienced. Donghua failed to break through many times because of them. However, H. Kirklen's midfielder had no use. The front line, except for the wings, was still presentable. Cooperation was extremely lacking. A plate of loose sand. The balls sent from left and right frequently could not be used. They could not attack the goal in front of the goal, and center forward Notte also did not have the skill to control the ball.

The Western Youth Association Launches International Volleyball Tournament 198

It is Predicted That China, Italy, Russia, America, and You Will Participate; A Circular System Will Be Adopted; Three Sets Will Be Fought Each Time. At a recent meeting, the Western Youth Association Volleyball Committee decided to launch the Zhizhi International Volleyball Tournament at the end of the second week of Western Youth Association volleyball. Athletes from various countries will organize one of the strongest teams to participate. It is predicted that five countries, China, Italy, Russia, America, and You, will join. A one-week system will be adopted, with three sets each time. The team with the most sets won will be the champion team and can participate for free. The second week of the Western Youth Association Group A volleyball competition was originally scheduled to be held once a week on Wednesdays. It is now scheduled to be held twice a week, once on Wednesdays and once on Fridays, so that it can be concluded as soon as possible, and the international volleyball tournament can be realized sooner.

The date is subject to the solicitation of Liu's personal opinions and a letter to the National Sports Association for assistance. (Beiping Correspondence) The Standing Committee of the Northeast Sports Association held a regular meeting in the conference room of the East University South School at 3:00 p.m. on the 29th to discuss matters related to the participation of various provinces in the Northeast in the Far East preliminary elections. The attendees included Wang Zhuoran, Hu Anshan, Pang Ying, Wang Lan, etc. Wang Zhuoran chaired the meeting, and Pang Ying recorded the minutes. When the meeting opened as usual, the discussion began. The following eight proposals were resolved. (1) The association's proposal to send Liu Changchun to Shanghai to practice (resolution): A letter was sent to the Chinese National Sports Association to inform the association that the association had sent athlete Liu Changchun to Shanghai to practice early, and to ask the National Sports Association to provide appropriate assistance. As for the date of departure to Shanghai, Liu Changchun's personal opinions will be sought first, and then the decision will be made. It was decided to appoint three committee members, Hu Anshan, Pang Ying, and Wang Lan, as the preparatory committee. Regarding the economy, funds will be allocated from the association's surplus annual expenses to subsidize it. (3) Whether to hold the spring games and sports meet as usual this year (resolution): The sports meet this year will be held in early May. The association will send letters to various middle schools in the Northeast to start practicing in advance and prepare to participate at that time. The ball games will be held at the end of March. (4) Whether to print the work report of the association's standing committee in the 22nd year (resolution): The work report for the 22nd year will not be printed separately, but will be published in the publication. (5) Whether to send letters to vocational middle schools in the Northeast, Fuguan Middle School, Northeast Middle School, Zhongshan Middle School, etc., inviting them to join the association (resolution): Letters will be sent to the schools inviting them to join the association. (6) The association's proposal to suggest to middle schools in the Northeast regarding the progress of physical education and the teaching methods to be implemented (resolution): It was decided to appoint Hu Anshan and Pang Ying to be responsible for handling it. (7) Whether to make the association emblem (resolution): The number of people is too small, so it will be postponed for the time being. (8) Whether the basketball teams from various provinces in the Northeast will participate in the Far East preliminary elections (resolution): A decision will be made after examining whether each school has elite athletes.

The women's race walk will also start from the Sports Field and end behind the Disabled People's Home, and will return to the Sports Field. Registration will begin on March 3rd, and the event will be held on the 11th. General Outline of the Reward and Punishment Methods for Middle Schools and Normal Schools in Zhejiang Province 207

The Ministry of Education has approved the general outline of the reward and punishment methods for middle schools and normal schools and the examination method for moral conduct in vocational schools submitted by the Zhejiang Education Department for the record. Its reward and punishment methods are sufficient to encourage students to enter the right track. The general outline is recorded below. (A) The types of rewards are as follows: (1) Scholarship, (2) Medal,

(Prepared by the Education Department, Zhejiang Provincial Middle School Student Medal, each school)

Filed for the record. (3) Certificate, (4) Registration of good deeds (merit or moral conduct bonus points), (5) Verbal encouragement. (B) The types of disciplinary actions are as follows: (1) Expulsion, (2) Order to withdraw from school or suspension, (3) Probation (staying in school under observation), (4 Warning) or demerit, (5) Suspension of leave or reprimand. (C) Students who meet one of the following items will be rewarded: (1) Those whose moral conduct, academic performance, and physical education performance are all

Excellent. (2) Those who are diligent in learning and have perfect attendance throughout the semester. (3) Those who live appropriately. (4) Those who have special good deeds. (5) Those who are enthusiastic in service and have achievements. (6) Those who are diligent in labor and have achievements. (7) Those who handle accidents appropriately. (8 Other. (D) Students who commit one of the following items will be punished: (1) Those whose words and deeds are perverse, whose character is bad, and who are incorrigible. (2) Those who damage the school's customs, discipline, or reputation. (3) Those whose moral conduct is rated D. (4) Those who do not abide by school rules. (5) Those who do not obey education. (6) Those who insult classmates. (7) Those who have bad habits or behaviors. (8) Other. (E) Each school should formulate its own reward and punishment rules in accordance with the provisions of this general outline and submit them to the Education Department for approval and implementation.

British American Tobacco Factory Interferes with Administration of Workers' Children's School 210

The Labor Union Held an Emergency Representative Congress Yesterday, Submitting a Petition to Party, Government, and Educational Organizations to Prevent It. The Shanghai Fifth District Cigarette Industry Labor Union, recently due to the factory's interference with the administration of workers' children's schools, undermining labor education, has had disputes. At 5:00 PM yesterday, it convened an emergency representative congress to discuss countermeasures and submitted a petition to party, government, and educational organizations, to prevent the factory's illegal behavior. The details are as follows:

Emergency Meeting The Fifth District Cigarette Industry Labor Union held an emergency representative meeting at its headquarters at 5:00 PM yesterday. More than one hundred representatives attended. Lu Yinchu, a representative from the municipal party headquarters, and Wang Gang, a representative from the social affairs bureau, publicly elected Chen Peide as chairman and Sun Xiaozhu as recorder. First, the chairman reported on the factory's undermining of the school, followed by resolutions: (1) Petitioning party, government, and educational organizations to prevent the factory's illegal behavior. (2) Issuing a notice to workers. (3) Advising the company's board of directors and factory director. (4) Preventing lackeys from entering the factory to provoke animosity between labor and management. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Petition The main points of the union's petition to party, government, and educational organizations are as follows: (1) Article 4 of the school agreement stipulates that the school's administrative finances are the responsibility of both labor and management, and neither party shall directly interfere. During the last winter vacation, the factory notified workers' children that they must register with the factory, which exceeded the scope of the agreement. The union had previously submitted a petition to correct this. This year, students must be admitted with a copper plate issued by the factory, and it is strictly stipulated that only the factory workers’ own children are allowed to attend. All relations such as grandparents and grandchildren, uncles and nephews, brothers, and sisters, are rejected. This has caused the grandchildren of elderly female workers, and the younger siblings and nephews of unmarried female workers and unmarried male workers to have a reason to sigh. The school did not comply, so the factory threatened to cut off funding. Viewing this unreasonable and reckless behavior, it sets a bad precedent in the education field. This is the first point of interfering with school administration and undermining labor education. (2) Since the appointment of Principal Shen Yu in the previous term, he has been enthusiastic about education. Because the factory wanted to place a private individual, it opposed Principal Shen fiercely, hindering him in every way. The private individual they wanted to place was Ge, who had been accused and dismissed by the municipal education bureau. It is even more obvious that they are trying to carry out the will of the other party and carry out illegal actions. This is the second point of interfering with school administration and undermining labor education. (3) The school's funds are customarily received from the factory in two installments each month, which is clearly stated in the old agreement. However, the factory has not yet issued the school's funds for August and September of the previous term, and plans to arbitrarily dispose of them, causing difficulties for the previous board of directors to complete the handover. This is the third point of interfering with school administration and undermining labor education. (4) At the school's board of directors meetings, five factory directors attend, but difficulties arise every time the board's resolutions are implemented. The reason for this is that the factory refuses to comply, resulting in many resolutions being made but not implemented. Therefore, the chairman has the intention of withdrawing, and the school is in danger of disintegration. This is the fourth point of interfering with school administration and undermining labor education. The above points are all recent facts of the factory. The factory claims to want to improve the school, but it is doing the opposite. If they do not want to improve it, it is unknown what kind of state it will reach. The union feels obliged to break its silence and hereby petitions your government to order the factory to cease its illegal behavior immediately, and to appoint an experienced principal to preside over school affairs to maintain education.

The exhibition displayed more than five hundred works by teachers and students of the academy, such as Chinese paintings by Lin Fengmian, Jiang Danshu, Qi Baishi, Pan Tianshou, and Li Kuchan; oil paintings by Wu Dayu, Li Chaoshi, Lin Fengmian, and Cai William (Cai Yuanpei's daughter); sculptures by Liu Kaiqu; designs by Lei Guiyuan; and practical design by the students of the academy. Visitors all praised each other, praising their profound attainments and their ability to shine in China's art world. The exhibition will last for one week, with next Friday (the 9th) being the last day. Art lovers should hurry to see it. Today is a regular holiday, and the number of visitors will surely be even more enthusiastic.

In November, there were 7,281 men, 108 women, for a total of 7,389. In December, there were 6,865 men, 35 women, for a total of 6,900. The total number of readers throughout the year was 88,823, of which 44,334 were reading novels and magazines. It is also known that the total number of readers in January of 1934 was 6,403, including 3,668 from the academic community, 68 from the political community, 183 from the industrial community, 1,622 from the business community, 37 visitors, and 831 others. Bank Society Held Silver Price Discussion Meeting Yesterday 216

Bei Songsun Attended and Gave a Speech The Bank Society held a silver price discussion meeting at the Hong Kong Road Bank Club at 6:30 PM yesterday. More than one hundred members attended, including Xu Peikun, Li Zhaozhao, and Zhu Boquan. Bei Songsun of the National Bank, Gu Jigao of the Zhongfu Bank, and Westerner Kahn were invited to attend. The meeting was chaired by Zhu Boquan. After the meeting, Chairman Zhu reported first, and then introduced Bei Songsun, Gu Jigao, Kahn, and others to speak in succession. They all believed that the US government will raise the price of silver, and its domestic panic is the same as the phenomenon of gold price skyrocketing and silver price plummeting several years ago. However, we are not absolutely opposed to the US government raising the price of silver. If the degree of silver price increase is equal to the degree of price increase, and the silver currency is in a stable state, it is exactly what China is seeking. Now the United States is raising the price of silver in an attempt to dump American goods in other countries, regardless of the issue of prices. This policy will not only fail to succeed, but also affect the Far East trade market. China is a silver-using country, and the only countermeasure at present is to stabilize domestic currency prices, implement a silver export tax, or prohibit silver exports when necessary. Then, members expressed their opinions, and the discussion on the root cause and treatment methods of the silver price problem was very detailed. Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

The Spirit of Creation 218

— Han Yu

Children! Do you have a spirit of creation and experience in creation?

When you are playing with your friends or classmates, can you create other kinds of games besides the usual hide-and-seek and human pyramid to make everyone feel interested? This is the spirit of creation.

Children! Don't underestimate the spirit of creation. Inventors in the world all have a spirit of creation before they can invent things. Edison in the United States was originally a newsboy, but he had a great spirit of creation. So he successively invented the electric light, telephone, and phonograph for us to use.

Children! Now is the time for you to practice the spirit of creation and experience. Don't underestimate the creation of games, because this is the best opportunity to practice the experience of creation. You must use the spirit of creation to cultivate the experience of creation at any time and any place. Then, it is not extremely difficult for you to become an Edison.

About Imitation 219

— Jun Si

Children, don't you often like to imitate the actions of adults, or imitate the characters in the play after watching a play? Here, I tell you that this is exactly the natural expression of your inner rich imitation. According to research, this imitation is the universal psychology of children, so if your parents or teachers understand child psychology, then they will definitely not interfere or prohibit your actions, because forced prohibition will be harmful to your physical and mental health.

However, children, you should pay attention! The real society is so flawed, and your future is full of traps, so your imitation should be so serious; the actions of adults are not all right, such as smoking, drinking alcohol, gambling, etc., are all unfavorable to you, and even historical figures have many wrong behaviors. Here, you should imitate their strengths and abandon their weaknesses. Naturally, for all imitations, you should carefully consider them beforehand. Imitation is not a bad thing. For example, Japan, although it is a militaristic country and our enemy, its ability to become strong and occupy an important position in the world is also derived from imitating Germany before the European War!

Emphasize Experimentation 220

— Jin Xi

I am very sorry to serve you cold coffee. The host apologized to Franklin.

"It doesn't matter!" However, it was just brewed, why did it get cold in a moment? Franklin asked suspiciously.

"Ah, that's because my servant is too lazy." The host replied. "For a long time, this cup has not been cleaned. The color is dark, and the brewed tea is colder than usual."

The host's response gave Franklin another speculation, he thought of the snow pile outside the window.

When he returned home, Franklin covered a piece of white cloth and a piece of black cloth on the snow. After a long time, he opened the two pieces of cloth to see. The snow under the black cloth had melted completely, and the snow under the white cloth had only melted half.

Franklin proved in the experiment the principle that "white repels heat and black absorbs heat."

My little friend in Shanghai, Brother W, it has been several months since I separated from Can last winter, I miss you very much!

In the cold winter weather, all the flowers are withered or dead, only the plum blossoms can stand tall and release fragrant flowers to resist the cruel wind and snow. It is truly worthy of being our national flower!

Our Suzhou Deng Wei has long been famous for producing plum blossoms. Everyone knows the three words "Fragrant Snow Sea." Now, when the plum blossoms are in full bloom, looking from afar, in the middle of a white color like snow, there are many red plum blossoms and green plum blossoms, which reflect each other. It is really pleasing to the eye and refreshing, and the spirit is excited. Generally, literati and elegant scholars all love plum blossoms. Plum blossoms are indeed the best of flowers.

The weather has been warmer recently, and all the flowers have gradually shown a resurrected form, with delicate buds on the branches, and the spring breeze is also very warm. This is a good day for playing!

The Owl's Relocation 222

— Dong Lin

The pigeon saw the owl living in the same forest busy preparing to relocate, and curiously asked it, "Why are you relocating?" The owl angrily replied, "The people living nearby all hate

my call, so I have to leave here and go somewhere else!" After the pigeon heard its words, it couldn't help but laugh, and advised it, "Wherever you move to, the people nearby will hate your call. Unless you correct your call, relocation is in vain!"

One's own shadow will follow you everywhere. It is a very pitiful act to blame the curvature of the shadow without seeking to correct oneself. However, there are many such people in this world! Children, let us avoid this problem from an early age!

What is the Reason for This? 223

— Ren Wei

Mom took a blue flower bowl and put it in the center of the table, and put a small copper coin in the bowl, and said to her ten-year-old daughter Lingmei, "Lingmei! you

come over! There is a very fun thing for you to see, and it can also increase your scientific knowledge. Stand next to the table and don't move! Is there anything at the bottom of this bowl?" Lingmei was short, so naturally she couldn't see the copper coin at the bottom of the bowl, so she replied, "Mom! I didn't see anything." Mom said, "There is a coin at the bottom of this bowl, now that you can't see it, it's because your body is too low. But I have a way to make you see the coin at the bottom of the bowl without moving the bowl closer to you, or tilting the bowl, or making your feet stand higher...." Lingmei looked suspicious and said, "Mom, I don't believe it!" Mom smiled and didn't speak, but saw her slowly pouring a bowl of water into the bowl. Strangely, a small copper coin suddenly appeared in Lingmei's eyes.

Lingmei ran over and pinched the corner of Mom's clothes, and asked Mom with a more suspicious look, "What is the reason for this?" Mom gently stroked Lingmei's little hand and said, "Lingmei, I'm giving you this toy"

is to let you know the reason for it. This is because light originally travels in a straight line, but when it passes through water, it changes its straight direction, so adding water makes it possible to see the copper coin at the bottom of the bowl."

Kuang Heng is poor, Kuang Heng is poor, but he studies hard, and the books are always in his hands. He wants to study but can't, who is willing to send the lamp!

It happened that the neighbor was a rich man, lighting the lamp and shining. Kuang Heng thought, and figured it out, so he chiseled a hole in the wall to borrow some light to use. Ah! Borrow some light to use.

Alas! Why don't children with lights study hard?

Xue Er 226

— Xu Luo

There was a child named Xue Er. When he was born, the doctor told Xue Er's mother not to let Xue Er get close to hot places, because he would die when he got close to hot places. Therefore, Xue Er's mother never allowed Xue Er to get close to hot places. One day, Xue Er insisted that his mother tell him how he was born? The mother said, "Xue Er, you... are part of my body. One day, Mr. Sun dried me, so part of my body turned into very light water vapor and flew into the sky like a bird, playing in the sky every day. One day, it was very cold in the sky, so it turned this water vapor into you

, and Mr. Wind brought it down." Xue Er listened and went to tell the other children.

The other children all liked Xue Er very much, because Xue Er was very beautiful, his face was very white, and his body was very cold, which was different from the rest of the children. Xue Er often caught very bad bugs in the field, so the children's parents also liked Xue Er very much.

One day, the children were all happily dancing around the fire. Xue Er saw it and ran over quickly. But as soon as he got close to the fire, Xue Er died.

Children's Play Life 227

— Shao Wen

Children are all very innocent. Their brains are like a blank sheet of paper, with nothing on them. But they all like to work and like to imitate everything they see and hear. This is expressed in their actions as games. Therefore, children's play is the beginning of their acquisition of knowledge. Parents and child educators should pay special attention to children's play life. Educating them in this way is more effective than educating them with textbooks in a rigid way.

In guiding children's play life, the most important thing is to cultivate their scientific knowledge. For example, when they are bouncing a ball, they should be told why the ball will bounce when it is patted on the ground. When they are driving a small car, they should be told some knowledge about cars. As for those boring games that cannot give children any knowledge, they should not be allowed to do them.

Educating children in play life is the best method of child education. We oppose all tendencies to despise children's play.

My Diary 228

— Wang Qianchuo

(1) January 3rd Today is my birthday. In the morning, my father wanted to go to the market to buy toys as a birthday gift for me. I said to my father, "Dad! Please don't buy it." My father asked me why? I said, "Because I think of the children in Northeast China, who are now living a painful life, and some can't even get enough to eat, so I don't want to enjoy myself." My father praised me very much after hearing my words.

(2) January 7th Today in botany class, Mr. Xu talked about "tree rings" and said, "We saw a tree trunk, and count the number of rings on it, and we can know how old the tree is." I found this very interesting after hearing this. But I didn't understand the reason, so I asked the teacher again. The teacher said, "The growth of the tree" is entirely due to the sap growing there. The part where the sap is located is in the middle of the bark and the heartwood. The sap surrounds the heartwood and grows, growing a ring every year. These rings are called annual rings. So we count the annual rings of a tree, and we know how old it is." After hearing this, I suddenly understood. It can be seen that as long as you are willing to ask more questions in learning, you will definitely understand.

Savings 229

— Recipient Society

Little friends, do you have any savings in the bank? Don't you think that only people save money? But if you think so, then you are wrong. Because animals also save money. Now let me tell you a few examples...

1. Bees collect honey from flowers and store it in their hives for when it is cold in winter and they cannot find food.

2. Camels live in the desert, and because it is not easy to find water in the desert, they often store water in the two humps on their backs (or one hump). So even when they cannot find water, it doesn't matter.

The above are two kinds of animals that can save. Below, I will talk about a plant that has the instinct to save.

3. Radishes usually store nutrients little by little in their roots. These roots are the radishes we usually eat, which serve as fertilizer for the seeds to germinate in the future.

Little friends! If there is anything you don't understand or don't believe in what I have said, you can ask your dear parents.

Animal Sleep 231

— Student Fan

Little friends, after reading books all day, and playing hard when you are free, aren't you very tired and need to sleep at night? If you are not allowed to sleep, you will definitely feel uncomfortable. Why is this? Because a person's brain cannot be used continuously all day long. After using it all day, it must have several hours of rest. This rest is sleep. However, rest should not be too long. For you children, ten hours of sleep is enough. For adults, eight hours of sleep is enough.

Sleep is not a special need for humans. All kinds of animals need sleep. However, the sleeping state of other animals is very different from that of humans. Like us humans, when we go to sleep, we must sleep on the bed, flat and comfortable. But like horses, when they sleep, they stand on the ground with all four feet, and only close their eyelids. That is sleep. If humans were asked to stand and sleep, they would definitely fall. It is impossible. In addition, like bats, their sleep is even more special. They hang upside down from the beams with their two feet. This is how they sleep. Sleep is originally the most comfortable rest for the body. It is strange that bats hang their bodies upside down, which is considered the most comfortable! As for fish, it is simply impossible to tell what their sleeping state is like. Fish are very alert. As soon as we run to the edge of the fish tank, the fish quickly swim back and forth. Little friends, isn't it?

There are many other animals with particularly strange sleeping habits. I am afraid that this article will be too long, so let's talk about it next time.

Women's Garden

Women and National Defense 232

— Translated by Li Sheng

ELondonderryNntionnlRfficiencyTheNineteentllCentrfyandatersanrary1934. The author, Ms. Londonderry, is the head of the largest women's organization in modern Britain, the "Women's Army." Although she is only a narrow-minded nationalistic heroine, she has 40,000 organized and strong women who follow her lead. This shows her extraordinary spirit and the great influence on British national defense. This article describes the past and present powerful activities of British women's organizations in national defense, and is clear and interesting. In this autumn of tense international situation, it can serve as a wake-up call for the drunken and dreamy ladies and gentlemen in our country, and can also serve as a mirror for new women with a sense of the times. It can also sweep away the concept of men's contempt for women. Therefore, it is specially translated to enrich this garden. However, due to space constraints, only a few places have been deleted. Translator's note.

World War I and Women. The World War I is liberating women in the belligerent countries from the last economic bondage to men. During the war, they were assigned various important tasks that they had never done before. And no matter how biased against women, one must admit that, in general, they fulfilled their tasks without any regrets. The occupations they engaged in were varied, and often involved complex difficulties that required special training, and they achieved greater success than men expected.

British women engaged in occupations such as nurses, pharmacists, massage therapists, cooks, reporters, military supplies manufacturers, messengers, drivers, etc. Many of them were awarded medals for their contributions. After the war ended, their groups were given words of gratitude by the King, Queen, or Queen. The achievements of British women's training at that time still remain. That is to say, British women are now able to work and have more independence than in any past era. Furthermore, they have a spirit of striving towards machinery and aviation. What is especially gratifying is that the spirit of cooperation has developed due to wartime activities. This spirit is manifested in various aspects of society.

Women and Organizations. Since the war, women have become very outstanding organizers. They exert their powerful influence in deliberative bodies from the Parliament to the village council. In politics, they have shown that they can deal with the necessary attention to detail to achieve success; at election time, they serve as greeters, persuaders, and speakers to exert their abilities. Many of them do city, street, and village leaders, which has greatly won the favor of the people. Especially in terms of their diligence and efficiency, they only exceed men. In higher occupations, since they were promised to join, they have been beneficial and harmless in various places. They now also participate in the affairs of banks and insurance companies. There are also many who work as architects, lawyers,

and doctors. There are also administrative officials and police officers. Women can also be seen in the executives of major newspapers.

Women's professional training. Ms. Pelia, Mullison, and Ge Lai became famous as aviators. Miss Bama Jieli. Fuchs Tu, who is engaged in chicken farming, competed with many men in the Bishi Lai shooting range and won the victory, and won the King's Medal. Mrs. Hainai. Normanton registered as a lawyer belonging to the High Court and fulfilled her duties, proving that married life is not adversely affected by this. There are also many women who serve as judges, and they are especially suitable for judging juvenile cases. They have sympathy and understanding, so they cannot do without them. They serve as visiting judicial officers and are responsible for inspecting the lives and treatment of women in prisons, making great contributions to the country.

Since the war, women have undertaken various tasks as mentioned above. But it will not therefore forget the duty of women as conservatives worry. They will not lose common sense and sound judgment, just as they are working hard to remedy the physical weaknesses that are not as good as men. But most women do not tend to break away from the duties of family duties. I hope to leave the family easily, and I think that such a thing is not easy to do.

The current international relations. Now we cannot ignore the various signs appearing on the international horizon. In many ways, the current situation in Europe is very similar to the scene in early 1914. Although the Geneva International League has tried its best to seek international peace, relations between countries are still extremely tense. The international competition arising from the market competition has turned into political resentment, and this resentment has become more and more fierce due to the competition of armaments. Given the situation, the governments of all countries have trained their citizens in chemical warfare defenses such as the use of gas masks. My friends who recently inspected the two major continental European countries, Germany and the Soviet Union, said that both countries are practicing gas masks. In these two countries, synthetic ammonia and nitric acid are being vigorously manufactured under the name of fertilizers. Naturally, once in wartime, these items will be used to manufacture explosives and toxic gases, especially tear gas and blistering gas. The Soviet Union often uses airplanes to spread mobile fertilizers, which can also be used in combat, needless to say.

Women's organizations. Now no one wants a brutal war to occur, but at the same time no one can guarantee that it will not occur. At this moment, it is necessary to add some investigation to women's groups that have a close relationship with national defense. There are two women's bodies in Britain that deserve special attention. One is purely medical (the Association of Volunteer Women), and the other is the "Women's Army," which has a broad social mission. The latter is held by myself as chairman.

The Association of Volunteer Women was originally named TdeOrganizationofvoluntaryAidinEnglandandWales (British and Welsh Association of Volunteer Women), and was established in 1909 with the assistance of the War Department. The original purpose was to serve as a local medical institution in the country during wartime, and later it was sent abroad to assist the medical affairs of the Army, Navy and Air Force. When war was declared in 1914, the British

The Red Cross and the St. John's Association recruited as many as 2,000 detachments, with more than 70,000 personnel, and the number increased by half when the war began. Since 1923, its scope of activities has been further expanded. Now there are trained staff such as nurses, pharmacists, wireless telephone technicians, massage therapists, practical assistants, and opticians. There are ordinary cooks, clerks, and trainee nurses who are not yet mature in training. They are also divided into mobilized and non-mobilized classes. The mobilized class consists of women between the ages of twenty-one and forty, who are widely engaged in medical care and nursing for the national army at home and abroad in wartime. Their compulsory subjects are the theory and practice of nursing. The optional subjects are chemical warfare defense, hygiene, tropical hygiene, cooking, and childcare. Now, especially for the aforementioned reasons, special attention is paid to chemical warfare defense. Recently, an air rescue organization has been added. There are now three air ambulance classes. The Women's Legion (TheWomensleaion) was founded by me in 1915, and its purpose is to replace men who take up arms and go to the military for the country's benefit in times of crisis. Members wear yellowish-brown uniforms and receive regular and strict training. As many as 40,000 people have registered. I initially wanted them to engage in farming. Although farmers welcomed them, mocking anonymous letters were received from all sides at the time. Most of them said that the plan was simply ridiculous, and some said that the appearance of women marching in the streets in men's clothing

, It's too weird. The purpose of the patriotic women of the military country is not to form a team of martyrs or women's volunteer army. Women should do their duty to the country.

Tasks, not to replace men, do what men should do. Women are women, and they should not imitate men from places different from men. But there are many tasks that women should do for the country. The reason why I named it a women's army is because the term LEGION reminds me of the efficiency and training of the ancient Roman army. This is by no means from the perspective of the army. I think it should be regarded as the basis of a national life. In my mind, I feel that a trained and powerful women's state

Exist everywhere. From the beginning, I opposed the idea that all the work of women is compulsory. Therefore, in addition to organizers, committee members, and propagandists, I do not use voluntary personnel. I have always held the doctrine of replacing male labor with female labor. In order to maintain the necessary control and the high standard of operation, it is extremely necessary to pay the

Appropriate remuneration or handling fee is extremely necessary. This is what the members appointed by the Ministry of Military Affairs in November 1916 also considered necessary. They said that until the end of the war, about 80% of the labor in the United Kingdom was done by paid female workers.

The Women's Army and related groups. The Women's Army has made many contributions to the country during the war. The parent body of the side branches of the group. Those that can be called her detachments include the Women's Land Army, the Queen Manling Assistance Team, the Women's Navy, and the Women's Air Force. The main tasks of the Women's Army during the war were transportation, employment, cooking, etc. Later, the cooking aspect was taken over by the Queen Manling Assistance Team.

In addition to these military-related groups, the Women's Army also has detachments for all operations that women must perform, such as farming. However, they are doing their best to handle the most important operations such as transportation, such as the transportation of goods and wounded soldiers, and even the use of messengers. After the war ended, the Chief Accountant, Sha, John. Cowan praised the Women's Army's Transportation Department and said, "Without their help, the transportation work could not have been so complete and quick. Now they have become an indispensable element of the army." The Women's Army's Automobile Department still exists as a reserve transportation department.

The plan to create a new women's group. When necessary, women's groups can be expanded as much as possible. As recently reported in the newspapers, Commander Yaling wanted to organize a new group called the Women's Reserve Army. The purpose is to train the necessary wartime matters such as life-saving, defending against poison gas, cooking, and transportation. However, this seems to be repeating and conflicting with the work of existing groups.

The reform of existing groups. Therefore, I have to oppose the plan to organize new women's groups related to military affairs and advocate reforming existing groups, placing them under strict control, giving them new vitality, and dividing operations according to the scope of work to be done in the future. Now, it is the most appropriate time to transform the Women's Army to contribute to the country in the future. I think it is especially necessary to hold cooking lectures all over the country and train women in the knowledge and skills of chemical warfare defense, machinery management, and transportation and messengers of the Navy, Army, and Air Force.

Local activities. During wartime, there is a lot of assistance from women in cities and local areas. And the activities of women's groups are more convenient based on local areas. This will never conflict with the activities of the existing Red Cross, St. John's Association or branches of such groups. Because the Women's Army has far more members than any other women's group, it can cooperate with various groups as needed to perform the tasks of women for the national army. Lessons from the Great War. If there had been a fully trained women's assistance group when the Great War broke out in 1914, then there would have been no need to be so hasty. The situation of hastily recruiting nurses across the country, holding cooking lectures, and mixing up and down is still fresh in our memories. All of these require full preparation in peacetime. We have learned a great lesson from the Great War, and it is not okay to forget this lesson.

For the sake of national security, it is necessary for women to continue to receive the training they received during the war. These experiences should now be inherited by younger sisters. It is also the duty of women to do their best, individually or collectively, to protect the country in times of national crisis. Any country, when it is in danger of survival, is not enough to rely on the power of men alone, and a total national mobilization should be carried out. Then it is absolutely necessary for women to prepare actively, implement full training and organization in peacetime.

Madame Sanger, a World-Famous Woman 233

— Xue Wen

In 1922, a woman who advocated birth control came to our country, China. She was Madame Sanger, who went everywhere to promote a theory of protecting motherhood.

Her proposition of birth control, on the one hand, is to prevent excessive population, and on the other hand, is to protect the freedom of motherhood. According to her, it can save crime, famine, war, etc. in society, so it is also a method of improving society. Her various life situations from childhood to middle age are worth knowing. The following is a brief description:

(1) Childhood. She was born in Corning, New York. Her father was a sculptor full of imagination, and her mother gave birth to eleven children in total. She was the fifth child, and the family was not very wealthy in terms of economy in order to enable their children to achieve their aspirations for schooling.

When she was young, she often received strict teachings from her father. For example, "A person must have his own idea. For this ideal, we must make great efforts." So when he taught children, he often said, "You must have a dream or illusion now, and you must strive to realize that dream in the future." Madame Sanger often received such inspiration, so she knew the trend of life early in her childhood.

She also had a habit of taking care of people when she was a child. For example, when she saw sick cats and other domestic animals, she always

She went to treat them with all her heart. She was like a mother to the homeless children nearby, advising them not to cause trouble. When her companions were injured while playing, she went to wrap up the injured fingers. In short, she was like a nurse.

At that time, she also discovered a tragic fact, that is, many playmates, if they obtained labor certificates, would leave home and go to the factory to work. She carefully studied and knew that they could no longer receive education and had to go to the factory because there were younger siblings in the family and their parents were under economic pressure.

(2) Girlhood. After that, she boarded at a school to study. In this era, she liked sports very much, such as basketball, dancing, etc. She participated enthusiastically. There were more than 500 people in that school, and she and her classmates did various extracurricular activities. The most enthusiastic one was practicing speeches.

Once, she decided to give a speech on the necessity of women's suffrage, but when she practiced, she was ridiculed by her classmates.

, So it was very difficult. So, good secretly ran to

She spoke by herself, pointing and gesturing, in a place far away from the school. At this time, the audience and the lecturer were all her own. Later, she spoke in public at the assembly, which attracted everyone's attention. As a result, a group for the suffrage movement was organized. At that time, she was only fourteen years old.

Later, she went to New York Hospital to study for four years and graduated from the Medical Research Department. She liked internal medicine and nursing. In these four years, she witnessed the pain of production and death, so a kind of power was added to her thoughts.

(3) After marriage, after her medical studies ended, she married Sanger, who was studying art.

After her marriage, she continued to engage in nursing, which continued for fourteen years. During these many years, she witnessed that poor families suffered from having many children and were trapped in tragic

In the situation of a bitter life, therefore, she gradually felt that the necessary conditions for women's liberation were really a healthy body. No matter how lofty the ideal is, if one becomes a mother, nothing can be realized. Good also saw a poor woman who prevented pregnancy with a non-scientific method, but died of poisoning as a result. Therefore, she firmly believed that birth control must have scientific methods. In 1914, she promoted her propositions to the general public.

However, during her propaganda period, she was repeatedly accused. Once she was arrested and imprisoned, and she was released after many people tried to rescue her. There are more than 20 propaganda agencies she established in her country. She came to Asia for propaganda in 1922. When she arrived in Japan, she was initially stopped

, Later forced her not to preach that she could not land on the island, and arrived in our country from Japan, and gave several lectures in Beijing, Shanghai, Hong Kong and other places.

The Meaning of New Women 234

— Wen

Women account for half of mankind, and the other half are men. Originally, these two halves of mankind lived in the same society, and no problems would arise except for mutual production and mutual distribution. However, due to differences in living techniques and the heavy shackles of the patriarchal society built over thousands of years, women have come to be regarded as half of mankind that has become a problem today. The so-called "women's problem" that we hear today is really a great shame to the women's world as it is discussed and studied like "Jewish problem," "black slave problem" and special ethnic minority issues.

The common so-called "women's problem" is the problem of women's economic life. For thousands of years, the position of women in society has been a parasitic position. Because of the differences in living techniques, women can do nothing for society except to serve their husbands, take care of children, and handle family affairs. The economic life of society is completely controlled by men, while women lose their independence. But this kind of life can only be stable in the feudal society for thousands of years. When social changes occur at the same time as the changes in social economy, this kind of life must be eliminated. The so-called "women's problem" that we are discussing today is just occurring at the present stage when the huge feudal society is collapsing and the parasitic class is generally shaking. It does not occur at the stage when women were bought and sold as commodities in the heyday of feudal society. It especially proves that the women's problem is not a separate problem, but one of the overall social transformation problems. The solution to the women's problem cannot be solved alone. It must be solved in the overall solution of the social problem. The actual effect of the solution.

The status of women is indeed so unfortunate as determined by society and "innateness," but women themselves have destroyed their position in society, and the whole line has escaped from the ranks of independent life. Obviously, it should be blamed on women themselves. Let's take a look at the facts. We cannot understand the meaning of her existence in society and give up her obligation to fight for independent life. There are still many women who are willing to make a living under the slavery of men, and these women are especially all intellectual class and the bourgeois class, who claim to be enlightened. We must now re-estimate the definition of new women. New women must not only break free from the slavery of men in the family and become an important member, but also strive for social status and become an important member of society. These two are linked.

The responsibility for women's liberation rests on women themselves, and also on women's participation in actual social life and cooperative overall solutions to social problems.

Glimpses of Working Women's Lives 235

— Yi

Spring has arrived! A group of people with hopes of getting rich still have to live a life where it is difficult to get rich. Hundreds of thousands of working women, from spring to winter, from morning to night, from the countryside to the city, from home to the factory, who isn't busy because of the oppression of life? But people can only lightly know that they work for life, and often ignore how noteworthy and serious their lives under labor are.

No one can deny that human survival has many necessary conditions in life, such as rest, entertainment, hygiene, education... Especially for women, attention to physiological development in childhood, protection of maternal health in adulthood, and so on. Unfortunately, our female compatriots in the labor world are too far away from human life.

Workshops filled with the deafening roar of mechanical movements, rows of dim, pale yellow electric lights, sleepy-eyed, puffy-faced, weak-limbed women with dull eyes, either yawning while working in cotton mills or dozing off while working in silk mills, work from 6:00 PM to 6:00 AM the next morning. When the dancers are tired, the flying birds are also weary, the east is turning white, and the cars begin to move on the rails, they can then leave the huge factory in groups with heavy legs, dragging their limp bodies, braving the piercing wind, and return to their low and narrow homes. Then, feeding their children, cooking, doing needlework, washing clothes... At night, the suckling infants have to be carried around, subjecting their fragile nerves to the stimulation of the deafening sounds of the machines, and their weak respiratory organs breathe in large amounts of dirty air. If they are lucky, they can suckle their mother's nutrient-deficient milk and slowly grow up. "Life is hard in this life, we have to cultivate for the next life," a cotton mill worker in the dusty air of the workshop, takes out the cold leftover rice brought from home in a lunchbox, soaks it in the unfiltered hot water from the factory's hot water pipe, and swallows the pickled radish while explaining to her companion the reason for eating vegetarian food, even though they don't look at small fish and shrimps. If someone eats two salted duck eggs brought from home in a meal, this will attract everyone's attention and be surprised at how wasteful it is. Their usual vegetables are mostly stir-fried beans, pickled radish, soybean sprouts, pickled mustard greens, etc. Eating green vegetables and tofu is too expensive. Indeed, with their income, they naturally cannot eat better food, let alone whether the quality of the food meets the needs of the human body, not to mention that there are many working women who are waiting for a vegetarian meal.

Spring has arrived, the warmth of the spring breeze and the beauty of the spring scenery are enough to inspire people's wisdom, cultivate people's temperament, and invigorate people's spirit. Of course, nature is not biased and equally benefits working women, but they are not blessed to enjoy it. They don't ask about the flowers of spring, the moon of autumn nights, nor do they care about the rain of summer or the snow of winter. They just mechanically walk into the factory like ghosts under the streetlights every day, and suffer the heat attack of water vapor and car oil gas in the tall workshop without seeing the sun. Their mechanical life and fixed environment do not require any wisdom or thought. They only know that the price of rice has risen, and that wages have been reduced. When they get off work, they still walk home like ghosts under the streetlights.

Women's Garden's Current Work 236

— Mao Rui

In this tense and screaming atmosphere of natural disasters, man-made disasters, and national crises, suddenly our women's mentor is born to awaken the dreaming women of China. This is the gospel of our women's world, and also the gospel of the country and society! Everyone knows that since the "May Fourth" Movement, Chinese society has been filled with slogans of women's liberation, inheriting the legacy of European and American women's movements, but looking at the Chinese women's world today, has it been liberated to the path of light? A portion of knowledgeable women have already run from the countryside to the cities, running towards the path of modernization, dreaming sweet dreams of "love" and intoxicating the souls of the general youth.

In the countryside, most of the women are still oppressed and numb.

The result of Chinese women's liberation is the creation of many female customers who sell goods from the East and Southeast Asia, and characters in romance dramas. What we uniquely hope from the Women's Garden today is to awaken the modernized women of China and lead them to the countryside to awaken the women in the majority of rural areas who are oppressed and living the lives of cattle and horses. Let us all walk towards the bright road of women, to wash away the stain of modern Chinese women. This is the most urgent work in our Women's Garden!

Wheat Flour Prices: Morning Decline, Afternoon Rebound 246

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month showed a trend of initial stability followed by a decline. Due to the recovery in foreign wheat prices, with Chicago rising by five to six cents and Canada rising by about five cents, people were initially calm when the prices opened. However, as the bulls sold off and various factories gradually released their holdings, people became extremely weak again. For a time, selling was very active and market prices fell sharply. For example, the price for this month fell to as low as two yuan and four cents, and the price for June fell to as low as two yuan, one cent, and two and a half mills, a drop of twelve cents compared to the previous day. These low prices are a new record for this year. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was initially stable, but then gradually rebounded. Because the market was short, there was covering. After three sessions, there were rumors that the conflict between Japan and Russia was likely to become serious, so buying interest surged again. Whether this was a short squeeze is currently difficult to determine. As a result, the price for this month improved slightly by two and a half mills, the price for April and May remained unchanged, the price for June and July decreased slightly by five mills, and the price for August decreased slightly by seven and a half mills.

Near-Term Wheat Futures Firm, Distant Contracts Weak 247

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the market was relatively calm because the quoted prices for foreign wheat from Chicago and Canada had recovered by about five or six cents. In the near term, the market conditions tended to stabilize because the inventory of local wheat was not abundant and factories seemed to be holding back supply. However, for the distant months, the market was somewhat affected by the dumping of foreign wheat and the gradual decline in flour prices. The price for June fell to as low as three yuan and fifty-eight cents. The afternoon was slightly better. The price for July and August was consistently weak. As a result, the price for April improved slightly by two cents, the price for June improved by one cent, the price for July decreased slightly by two cents, and the price for August decreased slightly by three cents. The current wheat market price is stable and factory demand is still good. Bengbu wheat opened at three yuan, three cents, and eight cents, then fell to three cents and four cents. Xuzhou wheat was three yuan and four and a half cents. It is said that Fufeng and Huafeng purchased a total of 2,800 bags.

Rice Prices Fluctuate 248

Yesterday, the supply of rice from various sources to southern Shanghai was relatively abundant, with nearly 40 boats arriving (over 5,000 piculs). Late rice and various types of thick japonica rice each accounted for half. Customers from other provinces were actively purchasing late rice. As merchants from Tianjin and other places began to enter the market, the situation became tense, and sellers took the opportunity to raise prices, making the market seem to be on the rise. However, because buyers were unable to relax their grip, the price of over 2,000 bags of late rice from Qingjiao, Songjiang, Xisha and Lian areas rose by only five or six cents. However, judging from the trend, it seems to be changing. If the rise can continue for several days, there may be a turning point, given the domestic stockpiling. The market for various types of thick japonica rice was weak due to a decline in demand from shops. Fortunately, daily accumulation was not abundant, so there was no significant decline. For example, only the medium-grade Su Tong japonica rice fell slightly by five cents, while the high-grade rice was able to hold steady. However, the price of Changbang japonica rice fell by five cents to nearly one foot for both high and low grades due to limited sales channels. Due to the small amount of early rice arriving in Nanhang, the market showed a positive trend. Yangjian rice was still affected by the customer's sharp increase and fell by about ten cents. Dujian rice did not experience much change. Yinbian yuan rice supply exceeded demand, causing the price to fall by ten cents.

(Northern Shanghai) Approximately 27 or 28 boats arrived with various goods. The market saw a slight increase in demand. Premium grade broken japonica was stable, and lower-grade rice strengthened. Baiyuan early thin rice and Dujiangjian rice prices were stable. High-grade Yangjian rice was scarce and rose slightly by several cents, while medium and lower grades were stable and weak.

First Shipment of Bran and Flour to Tianjin for the New Year 249

Grain has always been the main export commodity from northern Shanghai, with flour being the most widespread. Since the end of the lunar month, merchants from various provinces have stopped purchasing due to year-end closing of accounts. Since the beginning of the New Year, most merchants from other provinces have not yet entered the market, resulting in no transactions. A large amount of flour was purchased by northern merchants the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the Yihua Guisheng ship transported 14,000 bags of flour to Yantai and Tianjin. Yesterday, the Taikoo Shengjing ship sailed to Tianjin, fully loaded with over 60,000 bags of flour and only a few hundred bags of rice. It is said that the Yihua Dingsheng ship will also export a large batch of flour to Tianjin next Monday.

The price of Niuzhuang soybean oil in the oil market fell by one and a half yuan. Yesterday, the price of soybean oil suddenly fell sharply. Traders were afraid of a major change after a long period of decline, so they opened a large market yesterday. However, sales were still limited to routine transactions. It is estimated that 1,600 units of Dalian oil were opened by ship (including goods for listening to the market), with a price of 9 yuan and 8 jiao, a sharp drop of 1 yuan and 1 jiao compared to the opening price. 700 units of Qishan oil were opened by ship, with a price of 9 yuan and 8 jiao, a drop of 9 jiao. 200 units of Qishan oil were opened by sand boat, with a price of 9 yuan and 8 jiao and a half, also a drop of 9 jiao. 150 units of Qishan Shahe oil were opened by ship, with a price of 10 yuan and 8 jiao, also a drop of 9 jiao. 300 units of Niuzhuang oil were opened by ship, with a price of 10 yuan and 7 jiao and a half, a significant drop of 1 yuan and 4 jiao and a half. 300 units of Niuzhuang oil were also opened by sand boat, with a price of 10 yuan and 8 jiao, a sharp drop of 1 yuan and 5 jiao.

First Trading Session of Hongjiang Tung Oil Begins 250

Every spring, Jiangxi tung oil merchants and customers negotiate the opening prices in Zhenjiang because the new goods are about to be listed. The prices of various brands have been negotiated and the market has opened. Regular Hong oils such as Jichanghe and Jiyingfeng, and Deputy Hong oils such as Qingyuanfeng, Yanghengyuan, Liutongqing and Xurongchang are being negotiated. Shanghai merchants purchase from Zhenjiang for about 4,000 to 5,000 barrels. However, Zhenjiang sells not only to Shanghai but also to Jiangbei, Suzhou, and other places, so the total number must be collected from all places. It is expected that sales numbers will be announced next week. However, sales this year may not be as strong as last year, and the amount of the first trading session is not expected to exceed last year, which can be foreseen. As new goods have arrived in Jinan in succession, Shanghai merchants will also begin wholesale sales. The price of Jichanghe for Regular Hong oil is around 27 yuan per barrel, Jiyingfeng is 26 yuan and 6 jiao, Yanghengyuan and Qingyuanfeng for Deputy Hong oil are still 23 yuan and 2 jiao, and Liutongqing and Xurongchang are around 23 yuan. Jifeng and Yingxiangtaifeng have been open for a long time, and the price is still 20 yuan and 4 or 5 jiao, and sales seem to be more focused on Xiangyun.

Yesterday, over 1,000 bags were sold again, with prices such as 11 yuan and 8 jiao for the first grade and 11 yuan and 5 or 6 jiao for Huanggangqing. Longjiangqing was particularly popular, with a sudden increase of 2 or 3 jiao to 10 yuan and 7 jiao and 5 cents and 10 yuan and 8 jiao. Zhuqing also rose by 2 or 3 jiao to 10 yuan and 8 jiao due to the influence of Chaoqing, with over 100 bags sold. Metal: Eastern White Iron Prices Frequently Decline 253

Eastern white iron prices have been declining recently. According to market surveys, this is due to the excessive amount of goods arriving. For example, the price of a 36-inch sheet is only 8 jiao and 7 cents (the price sold by Eastern trading companies), while the market price is 9 jiao and 1 or 2 cents. Large-scale transactions are also only sold for about 8 jiao and 8 or 9 cents. The price of a 37-inch sheet is 1 yuan, 4 cents, and 5 cents. For large purchases, the price can be as low as 1 yuan, 2 cents, or 3 cents. Transactions are more active than for 36-inch sheets. However, too many goods have arrived from Eastern small trading companies recently, which has also affected the market a lot. According to reports from the same merchants selling this product in the market, the future market situation is still very pessimistic due to the manipulation of Japanese and Russian bosses.
